--- FILE: BadgerLib\Accounts.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class Accounts
    {

        public static string GetAccountName(string server, int account_id)
        {
            return GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, account_id, "name", true);
        }



        public static string GetAccountNames(string server, IEnumerable<int> account_id,string separator = "+")
        {
            List<string> names = new List<string>();
            foreach (int account in account_id)
            {
                string name = GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, account, "name", true);
                names.Add(name);
            }

            return String.Join($" {separator} ", names.ToArray());
        }


        public static string GetAccountContacts(string server, int account_id)
        {
            return GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, account_id, "email", true);
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, int account_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAccounts a where a.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }

        public static int GetAccountIdFromName(string server, string account_name)
        {
            string sql = "select account_id from vAccounts where name = @account_name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_name", account_name);
            int account_id = q.ExecuteSingle<int>("account_id");
            return account_id;
        }

        public static string GetAccountShortName(string server, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select name from vAccounts where account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            string name = q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name");
            return name;
        }
        public static string GetAccountLongName(string server, string account_short_name)
        {
            string sql = "select name_long from vAccounts where name =@account_short_name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_short_name", account_short_name);
            string name_long = q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name_long");
            return name_long;
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllAccountDetails(string server)
        {             
            string sql = "select * from vAccounts";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetFlowAccountDetails(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select a.name, a.account_id, a.name_long from vAccounts a" +
                " where is_flow_investor = 1" +
                " order by name";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetTrustAccountDetails(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select a.name, a.account_id, a.name_long, case when a.is_flow_investor = 1 then 'Flow Investor' when a.is_securitization_account = 1 then 'Securitization' else 'Other' end [account type] " +
                " from vAccounts a" +
                " where is_flow_investor = 1 or is_securitization_account = 1" +
                " order by name";

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }
}

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class ApplicantHelper
    {
        public int applicant_id;
        public string first_name;
        public string last_name;
        public string ssn;
    }

    public class Applicants
    {
        public static ApplicantHelper GetApplicants(string server, int applicant_id)
        {
            DataTable tbl = Applicants.GetInfo(server, applicant_id);
            ApplicantHelper a = new ApplicantHelper();
            a.first_name = tbl.Rows[0]["first_name"] as string;
            a.last_name = tbl.Rows[0]["last_name"] as string;
            a.ssn = tbl.Rows[0]["ssn"] as string;
            return a;
        }

        public static DataTable GetApplicantInfo(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetApplicantInfo @asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        
        public static DataTable GetInfo(string server, int applicant_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vApplicants a where a.applicant_id = @applicant_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@applicant_id", applicant_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int GetNewApplicantID(string server)
        {
            
            
            string sql = "select max(id)+1 [next_id] from Applicants";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("next_id");
        }

        public static bool ApplicantExists(string server, string max_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_Check_For_Applicant @max_id, @p_Exists output, 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            int Exists = 0;
            q.AddParameter("@p_Exists|OUT", Exists);
            DataTable dt = q.ExecuteTable();
            bool ApplicantExists = false;
            string cool_data = "";
            if (dt.Rows.Count > 0)
                cool_data = dt.Rows[0]["ApplicantExcists"].ToString();

                bool.TryParse(dt.Rows[0]["ApplicantExcists"].ToString(), out ApplicantExists);
            return ApplicantExists;
        }

        public static bool MapExists(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vApplicantsEx a where a.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
        }

        public static int GetNewApplicantIDAndAssociate(string server,string asset_id,int applicanttype_id)
         {
            int next_id = GetNewApplicantID(server);
            InsertApplicant(server, next_id); 
            AssociateApplicantWithAsset(server, next_id, asset_id, applicanttype_id);
            return next_id;
        }

        public static void InsertApplicant(string server,int applicant_id)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Applicants (first_name) values (null )";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@applicant_id", applicant_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static void AssociateApplicantWithAsset(string server,int applicant_id, string asset_id, int applicanttype_id)
        {
            string sql = "insert into AssetApplicantMap (asset_id,applicant_id,applicanttype_id) values (@asset_id,@applicant_id,@applicanttype_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@applicant_id", applicant_id);
            q.AddParameter("@applicanttype_id", applicanttype_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static bool AssetIdExistsInMap(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select count(*) from AssetApplicantMap where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            int count = q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            return count > 0;
        }

        public static int GetApplicantFromAssetNoMap(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = @"select distinct app.id [app_id] from API_APPLICATION api_app 
            left join API_APPLICATIONPROFILE ap_pro on ap_pro.APPLICATION_ID = api_app.id and ap_pro.PROFILE_TYPE= 'applicant' and ap_pro.POSITION = 1
            left join API_PROFILE pro on pro.id = ap_pro.PROFILE_ID and pro.DELETED_AT is null
            left join Applicants app on app.email = pro.EMAIL
            join AssetApplicantMap aap on aap.applicant_id = app.id and aap.applicanttype_id = 1
            where api_app.EXTERNAL_ID = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("app_id");
        }

        public static void UpdateContact(string server, int applicant_id, string first_name, string last_name, string middle_name, double? phone, string email, DateTime? dob, string ssn,string suffix, string mailing_address_full, int? maritalstatus_id,string primary_address_1, string primary_city, string primary_state, string primary_zip, DateTime? date_of_death)
        {
            if(null != ssn && ssn.Length != 11)
            {
                throw new Exception("SSN Issue");
            }
            string ssn_last4 = null;
            if(null != ssn && ssn.Length >= 4)
            {
                ssn_last4 = ssn.Substring(ssn.Length - 4, 4);
            }
            string sql = "update Applicants set first_name = @first_name, last_name = @last_name, suffix = @suffix, middle_name = @middle_name, phone = @phone, email = @email, dob = @dob, ssn = @ssn, ssn_last4=@ssn_last4, mailing_address_full = @mailing_address_full, maritalstatus_id = @maritalstatus_id, primary_address_1=@primary_address_1, primary_city=@primary_city, primary_state=@primary_state, primary_zip=@primary_zip, date_of_death=@date_of_death where id = @applicant_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@applicant_id", applicant_id);
            q.AddParameter("@first_name", first_name);
            q.AddParameter("@last_name", last_name);
            q.AddParameter("@middle_name", middle_name);
            q.AddParameter("@phone", phone);
            q.AddParameter("@email", email);
            q.AddParameter("@dob", dob);
            q.AddParameter("@ssn<varchar>", ssn);
            q.AddParameter("@ssn_last4", ssn_last4);
            q.AddParameter("@suffix", suffix);
            q.AddParameter("@mailing_address_full", @mailing_address_full);
            q.AddParameter("@maritalstatus_id", maritalstatus_id);
            q.AddParameter("@primary_address_1", primary_address_1);
            q.AddParameter("@primary_city", primary_city);
            q.AddParameter("@primary_state", primary_state);
            q.AddParameter("@primary_zip", primary_zip);
            q.AddParameter("@date_of_death", date_of_death);

            q.Execute();
        }

        public static void ImportApplicantFromMax(string server, string max_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec sp_MAX_Badger_Import_Applicant_Table @max_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@max_id", max_id);
            q.Execute();
        }
    }
}

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Asset
    {
        public string _asset;
        public string _server;
        public Asset(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            _server = server;
            _asset = asset_id;
        }

        public double? origination_fee
        {
            get
            {
                return AssetHelper<double>("origination_fee");
            }
        }

        
        
        
        

        private T? AssetHelper<T>(string db_attribute)
        {
            return BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<T>(_server, _asset, db_attribute, true);
        }

        public void Populate()
        {
            
        }
    }
}

        public static object GetPricingModelVer(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select isnull(exchange_rate_calc_version, -1) as 'exchange_rate_calc_version' from API_APPLICATION a where a.EXTERNAL_ID  = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            object o = q.ExecuteSingle<int>("exchange_rate_calc_version");
            return o;
        }

        public static int? NumberDealsWithHomeowner(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select count(*) [#] from vAssets ass join AssetApplicantMap aam  on ass.applicant_id = aam.applicant_id where (ass.asset_id = @asset_id or ass.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id",asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("#");
        }

        public static string GetUPSFolderNameOnlyFromID(string server,long pipeline_id)
        {
            string full_path = BadgerLib.Assets.GetUPSFolderFulLPathFromMondayId(server, pipeline_id);
            string folder = Path.GetFileName(full_path);
            return folder;
        }
        public static string GetUPSFolderFulLPathFromMondayId(string server, long pipeline_id)
        {
            string path = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<string>(server, pipeline_id, "name");
            
            
            
            

            string search = "*" + path.Replace(" ", "*").Replace(" ", "*").Replace("\n", "*").Replace(".", "");
            string root = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalUPSFolderLocationBaseLocation(server);
            var folders = Directory.GetDirectories(root, search);
            if (folders.Length == 0)
                return null;
            string folder = Path.GetFileName(folders[0]);
            return Path.Combine(root,folder);
        }

        public static string LocalFolderLocation(string server, string asset_id,bool cache=true)
        {
            string base_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION_LOCAL, cache, true);

        public static string LocalStagingFolderLocation(string server, string asset_id, bool cache = true)
        {
            
            
            string base_location = @"C:\Users\%USERNAME%\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\00 - Operations\Document Custody\Staging\";
            base_location = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(base_location);
            string[] folders = Directory.GetDirectories(base_location, asset_id + " - *",SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            if (folders.Length == 1)
                return folders[0];
            string folder_name_only = Path.GetFileName(Path.GetDirectoryName(LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id, true)));

            folders = Directory.GetDirectories(base_location, folder_name_only, SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            if (folders.Length == 1)
                return folders[0];
            return null;
        }
        public static string FindUPSFolder(string server, string asset_id, bool cache,bool check_if_exists)
        {
            string base_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION_OPS_LOCAL, cache, true);
            string ups_active_folder = LocalFolderLocationInternal(server, asset_id, base_location, null, cache,true);
            if(null == ups_active_folder)
            {
                string won_base_location = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Operations - Documents\02 - Homeowner Files\03 - Closed";
                ups_active_folder = LocalFolderLocationInternal(server, asset_id, won_base_location, null, cache,true);
            }
            return ups_active_folder;
        }

        private static string LocalFolderLocationInternal(string server,string asset_id, string base_location,string asset_folder,bool cache,bool check_if_exists)
        {
            if(null == asset_folder)
                asset_folder = FolderNameOnly(server, asset_id,cache);
            if (null == asset_folder)
                return null;
            
            string full = Path.Combine(base_location, asset_folder.Replace("\n"," "));
            string location = UtilsLib.FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(full) + @"\";
            if(check_if_exists && !Directory.Exists(location))
            {
                long max_id = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<long>(server, asset_id, "max_id", true);
                
                long? pipeline_id = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<long>(server, asset_id, "pipeline_id");
                if (pipeline_id != 0) 
                {
                    string last = GetUPSFolderNameOnlyFromID(server, pipeline_id.Value);
                    if (null != last)
                        location = last;
                }
                else
                {
                    string address_1 = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "address_1", true).Replace("\n"," ");
                    string last_2 = LocalUPSFolderLocation(server,address_1);
                    location = last_2;
                }
                if (!Directory.Exists(location))
                    location = null;
            }
            return location;
        }

        public static string WebFolderLocation(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            
            
            
            
            string convention = GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "folder_location", true);
            string base_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION);
            string full = Path.Combine(base_location, convention);
            string location = UtilsLib.FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(full) + @"\";
            return Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(location);
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllHEIQueryPivot(string server)
        {
            
            string sql = "select lien_position,dbo.Bucket(a.credit_score,50,'0',0) [credit_score_bucket],dbo.Bucket(a.investment_payment,25000,'0,000',0) [investment_payment_bucket], dbo.Bucket(a.starting_home_value,150000,'0,000',0) [starting_home_value_bucket],a.* from vAssetsEx a";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable() ;
        }

        public static Query GetAllHEIQueryFilterQuery(string server,List<string> assets)
        {
            
            string sql = "select a.* from vAssetsEx a join @assets ass on ass.item = a.asset_id order by ass.item";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", assets);
            return q;
        }

            return q.ExecuteTable();

        public static DataTable BatchBadgerChecks(string server,IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,IETA eta)
        {
            DataSet results = null;

            foreach (string asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                DataTable single = BadgerLib.Assets.GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssues(server, asset_id, false, false, null, null);

                if (null == results)
                {
                    results = single.DataSet.Clone();
                    
                }
                results.Merge(single);
                if(null != eta)
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            eta.Complete();
            return results.Tables[0];
        }
        
        public static Query GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssuesQuery(string server,string asset_id,bool display_summary,bool detail_badger,bool include_closed, int? days_back, int? priority_level)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ConsolidatedMissingData @asset_id=@asset_id, @display_summary=@display_summary, @detail_badger=@detail_badger, @include_closed=@include_closed, @days_back=@days_back, @priority_level=@priority_level";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@display_summary", display_summary);
            q.AddParameter("@detail_badger", detail_badger);
            q.AddParameter("@include_closed", include_closed);
            q.AddParameter("@days_back", days_back);
            q.AddParameter("@priority_level", priority_level);
            return q;
        }

        public sealed class ColumnCacher
        {
            private static readonly Lazy<ColumnCacher> lazy = new Lazy<ColumnCacher>(() => new ColumnCacher());

            public static ColumnCacher Instance { get { return lazy.Value; } }

            public List<string> simple = new List<string>();
            public List<string> complex = new List<string>();
            public bool es_listo = false;
            private ColumnCacher()
            {

            }
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field,bool use_cache)
        {
            EnsureColumnsCached(server);
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.simple.Contains(db_field))
                return GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache);
            else
                return GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(server,asset_id,db_field,use_cache);
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsEx a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if(ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }

        public static void EnsureColumnsCached(string server)
        {
            
            if (!ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                string sql = "select * from vAssets a where 1=2";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.Execute();
                ColumnCacher.Instance.simple.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
                q.SetSQL("select * from vAssetsEx a where 1=2");
                q.Execute();
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
                ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo = true;
            }
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssets a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttributeCutoff<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsExCutoff a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }
        public static List<T> GetMultipleAttributes<T>(string server, string asset_id, IEnumerable<string> db_fields, bool use_cache)
        {
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            foreach(string db_field in db_fields)
            {
                T field = GetSingleAttribute<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache);
                list.Add(field);
            }
            return list;
        }

    }
}

        public static string GetUPSFolderFulLPathFromMondayId(string server, long pipeline_id)
        {
            string path = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<string>(server, pipeline_id, "name");
            
            
            
            

            string search = "*" + path.Replace(" ", "*").Replace(" ", "*").Replace("\n", "*").Replace(".", "");
            string root = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalUPSFolderLocationBaseLocation(server);
            var folders = Directory.GetDirectories(root, search);
            if (folders.Length == 0)
                return null;
            string folder = Path.GetFileName(folders[0]);
            return Path.Combine(root,folder);
        }

        public static string LocalStagingFolderLocation(string server, string asset_id, bool cache = true)
        {
            
            
            string base_location = @"C:\Users\%USERNAME%\Unlock Technologies\Asset Management - Documents\00 - Operations\Document Custody\Staging\";
            base_location = Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(base_location);
            string[] folders = Directory.GetDirectories(base_location, asset_id + " - *",SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            if (folders.Length == 1)
                return folders[0];
            string folder_name_only = Path.GetFileName(Path.GetDirectoryName(LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id, true)));

            folders = Directory.GetDirectories(base_location, folder_name_only, SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            if (folders.Length == 1)
                return folders[0];
            return null;
        }
        public static string FindUPSFolder(string server, string asset_id, bool cache,bool check_if_exists)
        {
            string base_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION_OPS_LOCAL, cache, true);
            string ups_active_folder = LocalFolderLocationInternal(server, asset_id, base_location, null, cache, check_if_exists);
            if(null == ups_active_folder)
            {
                string won_base_location = @"C:\Users\DanFoster\Unlock Technologies\Operations - Documents\02 - Homeowner Files\03 - Closed";
                ups_active_folder = LocalFolderLocationInternal(server, asset_id, won_base_location, null, cache,check_if_exists);
            }
            return ups_active_folder;
        }

        private static string LocalFolderLocationInternal(string server, string asset_id, string base_location, string asset_folder, bool cache, bool check_if_exists)
        {

            if (asset_folder == null)
            {
                asset_folder = FolderNameOnly(server, asset_id, cache);

                if (asset_folder == null)
                {
                    
                    string legacyFolder = BadgerLib.Closing.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "ups_folder_name", cache);
                    if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(legacyFolder))
                    {
                        asset_folder = legacyFolder;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
                            "Unable to resolve the OneDrive folder for asset '" + asset_id +
                            "'. Neither 'folder_name_ups' nor 'ups_folder_name' could be found. " +
                            "This suggests the asset's OneDrive folder is missing or has not synced locally. " +
                            "Please verify that the OneDrive folder exists under the expected base path '" + base_location +
                            "' and that your OneDrive client is fully synced.");
                    }
                }
            }

            string full = Path.Combine(base_location, asset_folder.Replace("\n", " "));
            string location = UtilsLib.FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(full) + @"\";

            if (check_if_exists && !Directory.Exists(location))
            {
                long max_id = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<long>(server, asset_id, "max_id", true);
                long? pipeline_id = BadgerLib.Pipeline.GetAttributeInternal<long>(server, asset_id, "pipeline_id");
                if (pipeline_id != 0)
                {
                    string last = GetUPSFolderNameOnlyFromID(server, pipeline_id.Value);
                    if (last != null)
                        location = last;
                }
                else
                {
                    string address_1 = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "address_1", true).Replace("\n", " ");
                    string last_2 = LocalUPSFolderLocation(server, address_1);
                    location = last_2;
                }
                if (location != null && !Directory.Exists(location))
                    location = null;
            }
            return location;
        }

        public static string WebFolderLocation(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            
            
            
            
            string convention = GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "folder_location", true);
            string base_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION);
            string full = Path.Combine(base_location, convention);
            string location = UtilsLib.FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(full) + @"\";
            return Environment.ExpandEnvironmentVariables(location);
        }

        public static DataTable GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssues(string server, string asset_id,bool display_summary,bool include_closed, int? days_back, int? priority_level)
        {
            var q = GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssuesQuery(server, asset_id, display_summary, true, include_closed, days_back, priority_level);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable BatchBadgerChecks(string server,IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,IETA eta)
        {
            DataSet results = null;

            foreach (string asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                DataTable single = BadgerLib.Assets.GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssues(server, asset_id, false, false, null, null);

                if (null == results)
                {
                    results = single.DataSet.Clone();
                    
                }
                results.Merge(single);
                if(null != eta)
                    eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            eta.Complete();
            return results.Tables[0];
        }
        
        public static Query GetConsolidatedDataIntegrityIssuesQuery(string server,string asset_id,bool display_summary,bool detail_badger,bool include_closed, int? days_back, int? priority_level)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ConsolidatedMissingData @asset_id=@asset_id, @display_summary=@display_summary, @detail_badger=@detail_badger, @include_closed=@include_closed, @days_back=@days_back, @priority_level=@priority_level";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@display_summary", display_summary);
            q.AddParameter("@detail_badger", detail_badger);
            q.AddParameter("@include_closed", include_closed);
            q.AddParameter("@days_back", days_back);
            q.AddParameter("@priority_level", priority_level);
            return q;
        }


        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field,bool use_cache)
        {
            CommonLib.ColumnCacher.EnsureColumnsCached(server, "select * from vAssets a where 1=2", "select * from vAssetsEx a where 1=2");
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.simple.Contains(db_field))
                return GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache);
            else
                return GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(server,asset_id,db_field,use_cache);
        }



        
        
        
        


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        


        public static T GetSingleAttributeComplex<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsEx a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if(ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }

        
        
            
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public static T GetSingleAttributeSimple<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssets a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            if (ColumnCacher.Instance.es_listo)
            {
                ColumnCacher.Instance.complex.AddRange(q.ColumnListFromTable);
            }
            return t;
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttributeCutoff<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsExCutoff a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttributePosition<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vAssetsPositionEx a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0)))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }
        public static List<T> GetMultipleAttributes<T>(string server, string asset_id, IEnumerable<string> db_fields, bool use_cache)
        {
            List<T> list = new List<T>();
            foreach(string db_field in db_fields)
            {
                T field = GetSingleAttribute<T>(server, asset_id, db_field, use_cache);
                list.Add(field);
            }
            return list;
        }

    }
}

        {
            string sql = "select sum(a.investment_payment) [funded_deals] from vClosingEx c join vAssets a on a.asset_id = c.asset_id where c.funding_date between @start and @end";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@start", start);
            q.AddParameter("@end", end);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<double>("funded_deals");
        }

        public static double? AssetsOnBS(string server, DateTime asOf,int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT   t.account_id, sum(t.net_oface) [inv_pmt] FROM     vTrades t WHERE    t.settle_date <= @asOf AND account_id = @account_id GROUP BY account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<double>("inv_pmt");
        }

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@begin", begin);
            q.AddParameter("@end", end);

        }


        public static T? BankDetailsEarliest<T>(string server, DateTime asOf, string return_col) where T : struct
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBorrowingBase b where b.earliest_day = 1 and asOf = @asOf";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<T>(return_col);
        }

        public static double? FRBEODBal(string server, DateTime asOf)
        {
            
            string sql = "select sum(f.closing_balance) [balance] from vFRBBalanceHistory f join vBankAccts b on b.account_number = f.account_number join (select max(load_id) [latest_load_id] ,account_number from vFRBBalanceHistory f where transaction_date <= @asOf group by account_number) l on l.latest_load_id = f.load_id and l.account_number = b.account_number where b.is_unlock = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<double>("balance");
        }
        public static void ClearBorrowingBaseQuery(string server)

            Database.DBCache.GetInstance().RemoveCache(q);
        }

        public static DataTable GetLargeNonClearEdgeTransactions(string server, List<long> frb_acct_id,double threshold)
        {
            string sql = "select TOP 100 load_time,transaction_date [date],transaction_description [description],AMOUNT, nice_name [account] from vFRBInvEx f join @accts a on a.item = f.account_number join vBankAccts b on b.account_number = f.account_number  and abs(net_amount) > @threshold  and transaction_description not like '%CLEAREDGE%' and transaction_description not like 'INTERNET TRANSFER %'order by f.transaction_date desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@accts", frb_acct_id);
            q.AddParameter("@threshold", threshold);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


    }

        public static async Task<DataTable> GetTrustees(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select t.* from vAssets a join vTrustees t on t.state = a.state left join vClosing c on c.asset_id = a.asset_id where a.asset_id = @asset_id and ((c.asset_id is not null and c.closingagent_id = t.vendor_id) or (c.closingagent_id is null))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            
            return await q.ExecuteTableTask();
        }

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@show_all", show_all);

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Credit
    {

        public static DataTable GenerateReportFile(string server)
        {
            Query q = new Query("BatchCreditReport.sql", server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static DataTable CreditScoreSummary_OLD(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            Query q = new Query("CreditScores.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

       
        public static void DoAllCreditThings(string server, int creditfile_id, DateTime pull_date,string pdf,string html)
        {
            List<string> assets = BadgerLib.Credit.GetAssetIdsFromCreditFile(server, creditfile_id);
            foreach (string asset in assets)
            {
                string credit_pdf = BadgerLib.Credit.GetFullPathOfCreditReportPDF(server, asset, pull_date);
                SavePDF(credit_pdf,pdf);

                string html_pdf = BadgerLib.Credit.GetFullPathOfCreditReportHTML(server, asset, pull_date);
                SaveHTML(html_pdf,html);
            }
        }
        public static bool SavePDF(string full_location,string pdf)
        {
            if (null == pdf)
                return false;

            UtilsLib.FileLib.CreateDirectoriesAsNeeded(full_location);
            if (File.Exists(full_location))
                File.Delete(full_location);
            byte[] bytes = Convert.FromBase64String(pdf);
            System.IO.FileStream stream = new FileStream(full_location, FileMode.CreateNew);
            System.IO.BinaryWriter writer = new BinaryWriter(stream);
            writer.Write(bytes, 0, bytes.Length);
            writer.Close();
            return true;
        }

        public static bool SaveHTML(string full_location,string html)
        {
            if (null == html)
                return false;
            UtilsLib.FileLib.WriteFileSmartly(full_location, true, html);
            return true;
        }

        public static int InsertUpdateCreditScore(string server, int? load_id, DateTime asOf, int? creditscore_id, int applicant_id, int score, int creditscoremodel_id,bool initial, bool api)
        {
            string sql = "exec InsertUpdateCreditScore @load_id=@load_id, @asOf=@asOf, @creditscore_id=@creditscore_id, @applicant_id=@applicant_id, @score=@score, @creditscoremodel_id=@creditscoremodel_id, @initial=@initial, @api=@api, @creditfile_id=@creditfile_id, @creditscore_id_new=@new_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", load_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@creditscore_id", creditscore_id);
            q.AddParameter("@applicant_id", applicant_id);
            q.AddParameter("@score", score);
            q.AddParameter("@creditscoremodel_id", creditscoremodel_id);
            q.AddParameter("@initial", initial);
            q.AddParameter("@api", api);
            q.AddParameter("@creditfile_id", null);
            q.AddParameter("@new_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            int new_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@new_id"]);
            return new_id;
        }
    }

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Custody

        public static async Task<string> UploadCollateralToWSFS_Async(string StrLocalDirectory, string StrRemoteDirectory)
        {
            string RetVal = "";

            if (!Directory.Exists(StrLocalDirectory)) return string.Format("Local Directory {0} Missing", StrLocalDirectory);

            var sessionOptions = new SessionOptions
            {
                Protocol = Protocol.Sftp,
                HostName = CommonInterfaces.Constants.WSFSHostName,
                UserName = CommonInterfaces.Constants.WSFSstringUserName,
                Password = CommonInterfaces.Constants.WSFSstringPassword,
                SshHostKeyFingerprint = CommonInterfaces.Constants.WSFSstringSshHostKeyFingerprint,
            };

            try
            {
                
                using (var session = new WinSCP.Session())
                {
                    
                    session.SessionLogPath = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), $"winscp-log-{Guid.NewGuid():N}.log");

                    
                    session.XmlLogPath = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), $"winscp-xml-{Guid.NewGuid():N}.xml");

                    
                    
                    

                    session.Open(sessionOptions);

                    TransferOptions transferOptions = new TransferOptions();
                    transferOptions.TransferMode = TransferMode.Binary;
                    if (!session.FileExists(StrRemoteDirectory))
                        session.CreateDirectory(StrRemoteDirectory);

                    TransferOperationResult transferResult;
                    transferResult =
                        session.PutFiles(StrLocalDirectory, StrRemoteDirectory, false, transferOptions);
                    RetVal = String.Format("Successful Transfers : {0} \n\n Failed Transfers : {1} ", transferResult.Transfers.Count, transferResult.Failures.Count);

                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                RetVal += System.Environment.NewLine + ex.Message;
            }

            return RetVal;

        }
        public static string RenameAssetDirectoriesForWSFS(string StagingDirectory)
        {
            
            
            

            string FTPDirectory = StagingDirectory + "\\WSFS_FTP";

            if (Directory.Exists(FTPDirectory)) Directory.Delete(FTPDirectory, true);

            if (Directory.Exists(StagingDirectory))
            {
                string[] directories = Directory.GetDirectories(StagingDirectory);

                Directory.CreateDirectory(FTPDirectory);

                string[] files = Directory.GetFiles(StagingDirectory);
                foreach (string file in files)
                {
                    string filename = Path.GetFileName(file);
                    string new_filename = filename;
                    if (!IsExcelExtension(filename))
                    {
                        int idx = file.IndexOf(" ");
                        if (idx > 0)
                            new_filename = file.Substring(idx + 1);
                    }
                    string new_file = Path.Combine(FTPDirectory, new_filename);
                    File.Copy(file, new_file);
                }


                foreach (string dir in directories)
                {
                    DirectoryInfo dir_info = new DirectoryInfo(dir);
                    string new_directoryname = dir_info.Name;
                    int idx = new_directoryname.IndexOf(" ");
                    if (idx > 0)
                        new_directoryname = new_directoryname.Substring(0, idx + 1);
                    new_directoryname = new_directoryname.Trim();
                    new_directoryname = Path.Combine(FTPDirectory, new_directoryname);
                    CopyDirectoryContents(dir, new_directoryname);
                }

            }
            return FTPDirectory;
        }
        public static int CopyDirectoryContents(string source_full, string target_directory)
        {

            if (Directory.Exists(target_directory)) Directory.Delete(target_directory, true);
            Directory.CreateDirectory(target_directory);


            DirectoryInfo source = new DirectoryInfo(source_full);
            DirectoryInfo target = new DirectoryInfo(target_directory);

            string[] files = Directory.GetFiles(source_full);
            foreach (string file in files)
            {
                string filename = Path.GetFileName(file);
                string new_filename = filename;
                string new_file = Path.Combine(target_directory, new_filename);
                File.Copy(file, new_file);
            }
            return files.Length;
        }

        private static bool IsExcelExtension(string filename)
        {
            bool ret = false;
            string ext = Path.GetExtension(filename);
            if (ext == ".xls" || ext == ".xlsx" || ext == ".csv") ret = true;
            return ret;
        }

        public static string GetFolderFormat(string server, int collatshipment_id)
        {
            DateTime asOf2 = GetShipmentAsOf(server, collatshipment_id);
            string folder_override = GetFolderOverride(server, collatshipment_id);
            if (!String.IsNullOrEmpty(folder_override))
                return folder_override;
            
            return asOf2.ToString("M.d.yyyy");
        }

        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)

        }

        public static T GetSingleAttributeFromShipment<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, int doc_id, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vCollatShipmentsEx a where a.asset_id = @asset_id and doc_id = @doc_id order by asOf desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
            
            
        }

        public static string GetSingleListAttributeFromShipment<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, int doc_id, bool use_cache,string separator)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vCollatShipmentsEx a where a.asset_id = @asset_id and doc_id = @doc_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            List<T> t = q.ExecuteList<T>(db_field);
            string ret_val = String.Join(separator, t);
            return ret_val;
        }

        public static void AddAssetToFile(string server, string asset_id, int collatshipment_id, int? foreign_id,int? doc_id,string filename)
        {

            BadgerLib.Custody.InsertUpdateAssetInShipment(server, collatshipment_id, asset_id, foreign_id,doc_id,filename, string.Empty);
        }

        public static string GetStagingAssetFullDirectory(string server, int collatshipment_id, string asset_id,bool create_if_needed)
        {
            string staging_base = BadgerLib.Custody.GetStagingBaseDirectory(server,collatshipment_id);
            long max_id = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<long>(server, asset_id,"max_id",true);

            string asset_staging_folder = BadgerLib.Assets.FolderNameOnly(server, asset_id,true);
            string asset_staging_folder_final = $"{max_id} - " + asset_staging_folder;
            string asset_staging_folder_full = Path.Combine(staging_base, asset_staging_folder_final);

            if (create_if_needed && !Directory.Exists(asset_staging_folder_full))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(asset_staging_folder_full);
            return asset_staging_folder_full;
        }

        public static void AddAssetIDHistory(string server, List<string> asset_ids,string note)
        {
            foreach (string asset_id in asset_ids)
            {
                if (asset_id.Contains("-"))
                {
                    string asset_id_old = asset_id.Replace("-", "*");
                    bool exists = AssetHistoryExists(server, asset_id_old);
                    if (!exists)
                    {
                        string sql = "insert into AssetIDHistory (asset_id,asset_id_old,note) values (@asset_id,@asset_id_old,@note)";
                        Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                        q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
                        q.AddParameter("@asset_id_old", asset_id_old);
                        q.AddParameter("@note", note);
                        q.Execute();
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        public static bool AssetHistoryExists(string server,string asset_id_old)
        {
            string sql = "select * from AssetIDHistory where asset_id_old = @asset_id_old";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id_old", asset_id_old);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

            string full_dir = Path.Combine(root_staging, folder);

        }

        public static void InsertUpdateAssetInShipment(string server, int collatshipment_id, string asset_id, int? foreign_id,int? doc_id,string filename_only, string notes)
        {
            bool exists = AssetExistsInShipment(server, collatshipment_id, asset_id, foreign_id,doc_id, filename_only);
            if (!exists)
            {
                
                AddAssetToShipment(server, collatshipment_id, asset_id, foreign_id, doc_id, filename_only, notes);
            }
            {
             
            }
        }

        public static string RemoveCollateralFromStagingDirectory(string server, int collatshipment_id, string asset_id)
        {

        public static void AddAssetToShipment(string server, int shipment_id,string asset_id, int? foreign_id,int? doc_id,string filename, string? notes)
        {
            string sql = "insert into CollatShipmentMap (collatshipment_id,asset_id,foreign_id,doc_id,filename,notes) values (@collatshipment_id,@asset_id,@foreign_id,@doc_id,@filename,@notes)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@collatshipment_id", shipment_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            q.AddParameter("@notes", notes);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static void RemoveAssetFromShipment(string server, int collatshipment_id, string asset_id, int? foreign_id, int? doc_id, string filename)
        {
            string sql = "delete from CollatShipmentMap where asset_id = @asset_id and collatshipment_id = @collatshipment_id and ((@foreign_id is not null or @foreign_id = foreign_id) or (@doc_id is not null and doc_id = @doc_id) or (@filename is not null and filename = @filename))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@collatshipment_id", collatshipment_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            q.Execute();
        }


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public static int CreateCollateralShipment(string server, DateTime? asOf, DateTime? shipDate,
                DateTime? updateTime, string updateBy, int collatshipTypeId, string niceName, string trackingNum, string notes, int? docCustodianId)
        {
            int next_id = Common.GetNextId(server, "collatshipment_id");
            string sql = "insert into CollatShipments (id, asOf, ship_date, update_time, update_by, collatshiptype_id, tracking_number, note, doccustodian_id) " +
                "  values (@id,@asOf, @ship_date, @update_time, @update_by, @collatshiptype_id, @tracking_number, @note, @doccustodian_id )";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@id", next_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asof", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@ship_date", shipDate);
            q.AddParameter("@update_time", updateTime);
            q.AddParameter("@update_by", updateBy);
            q.AddParameter("@collatshiptype_id", collatshipTypeId);
            q.AddParameter("@nice_name", niceName);
            q.AddParameter("@tracking_number", trackingNum);
            q.AddParameter("@note", notes);
            q.AddParameter("@doccustodian_id", docCustodianId);
            q.Execute();
            return next_id;
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllShipments(string server,bool show_all, int? daysback=0)
        {
            
            if (daysback == null) daysback = 0;

            Query q = new Query("exec dbo.CollatShipmentSummary @show_all=@show_all, @daysback=@daysback", server);
            q.AddParameter("@show_all", show_all);
            q.AddParameter("@daysback", daysback);
            DataTable dt = new DataTable();
            try
            {
                dt = q.ExecuteTable(); 
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                throw new Exception(ex.Message);
            }
            
            return dt;
        }

        public static bool AssetExistsInShipment(string server, int shipment_id, string asset_id,Nullable<int> foreign_id,Nullable<int> doc_id,string filename)
        {
            string sql = "select top 500 * from vCollatShipmentsEx cse where cse.asset_id = @asset_id and cse.collatshipment_id = @shipment_id and (@foreign_id is null or cse.foreign_id = @foreign_id) and (@doc_id is null or cse.doc_id = @doc_id) and (@filename is null or cse.filename_raw = @filename)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@shipment_id", shipment_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            q.AddParameter("@doc_id", doc_id);
            q.AddParameter("@filename", filename);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count != 0;
        }
        public static string PrepareDataFile(string server, IEnumerable<string> asset_ids,Nullable<int> collatshipment_id,bool spawn_when_done)
        {
            string folder = $"US Bank Data File {DateTime.Today:M.d.yyyy}";
            string staging = Path.GetTempPath();
            string staging_full = staging;
            if (null != collatshipment_id)
            {
                folder = BadgerLib.Custody.GetFolderFormat(server, collatshipment_id.Value);
                staging = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.DOC_CUSTODIAN_STAGE, true);
                staging = FileLib.FileLocationWithVariables(staging);
                staging_full = Path.Combine(staging, folder);
            }

            DataTable d = BadgerLib.Custody.GetCustodyFile(server, asset_ids);
            
            Fields f = new Fields(server, Database.FieldHelper.GetFieldTableInternal);
            
            string file = UtilsLib.Excel.CreateQuickExcel(folder, new DataTable[] { d }, true, Excel.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.XLSX, false,f);
            
            
            
            if (!Directory.Exists(staging_full))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(staging_full);


            string full_file = Path.Combine(staging_full, folder + ".xlsx");
            if(spawn_when_done)
                FileLib.SpawnProcess(staging_full, true);
            
            
            
            
            
            
            
            return full_file;
        }

            q.AddParameter("@collatshipment_id", collatshipment_id);

        }

        }

        
        public static void SpawnIssueMail(string server, string asset_id, string exception, string notation, string data_file_full_location)
        {
            
            int vendor_id = 10;
            string to = BadgerLib.Vendors.SupportEmail(server, vendor_id);
            string cc = BadgerLib.Vendors.EmailCC(server, vendor_id);

            string nice_name = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "name_simple", true);

            string subject = $"#{asset_id} - {nice_name} | Collateral Question - Exception SAK: {exception} | {notation}";
            if(String.IsNullOrEmpty(exception))
            {
                subject = $"#{asset_id} - {nice_name} | Collateral Question";
            }
            


            string body = $"Team,<br><br><br><br><br>Thank You.";
            UtilsLib.Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, new string[] { data_file_full_location }, to.Split(';'), cc.Split(';'), null, true, true,null,null);
        }

        public static void SpawnAnnouncementMail(string server, int collatshipment_id)
        {
            
            int vendor_id = 10;
            List<string> attach_files = new List<string>();

            string ActiveDocCustodian = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.DOC_CUSTODIAN_NAME, true);
            string FundingSource_ShortName = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.FUNDING_SOURCE_WSFS, true);
            string FundingSource_LongName = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountLongName(server, FundingSource_ShortName);


            if (ActiveDocCustodian == "WSFS") 
            { 
                vendor_id = 20;
                string file = BadgerLib.Custody.GetFolderFormat(server, collatshipment_id);
                file += "." + Excel.EXCEL_FILE_FORMAT_SIMPLE.CSV.ToString();
                string staging_dir = BadgerLib.Custody.GetStagingBaseDirectory(server, collatshipment_id);
                string full_csv = Path.Combine(staging_dir, Path.GetFileName(file));
                attach_files.Add(full_csv);
            }

            string to = BadgerLib.Vendors.SupportEmail(server, vendor_id);

            
            DateTime asOf = BadgerLib.Custody.GetSingleAttribute<DateTime>(server, collatshipment_id, "asof", false);
            string folder = BadgerLib.Custody.GetFolderFormat(server, collatshipment_id);
            double? total = BadgerLib.Custody.GetTotalInvPmtInShipment(server, collatshipment_id);
            string subject = $"New Collateral - Unlock Partnership Solutions - {folder}";
            
            string cc = BadgerLib.Vendors.EmailCC(server, vendor_id);

            var names = GetNamesInShipment(server, collatshipment_id);
            string names_nice = String.Join("<br>", names);
            string callsign = BadgerLib.Users.GetCurrentUserAttributes<string>(server)?["callsign"];
            

            string body = $"Team,<br><br>We attest that the electronic files uploaded to this FTP folder, <b>{folder}</b>, are a true, complete and correct copy of Asset Files listed in the attached.<br><br></b><br><b><u>Collateral:\t\t${total:0,###}</b></u><br>{names_nice}<br><br>Please let me know of any issues.<br><br>Thanks,<br>-{callsign}";

            UtilsLib.Mail.CreateOutlookMail(subject, body, attach_files, to.Split(';'), cc.Split(';'), null, true,true, null, null);
        }

        public static int GetDocCustodianId(string server, string docCustodianName)
        {
            
            string sql = "select v.id from dbo.Vendors v join dbo.VendorTypes vt on vt.id = v.vendortype_id and v.vendortype_id = 5 where UPPER(v.name) = UPPER(@docCustodianName)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@docCustodianName", docCustodianName);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();


        }
    }

        public static DataTable DebtSummary(string server, string asset_id, int paid_off_at_origination)

        public static DataTable GetLienData(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select d.lien_position [lien #], d.balance [balance], d.lender_name [lender], d.asof [As Of], d.debt_type [debt type], d.cr_balance [cr mapped balance], d.account_open_date [account open dt] from dbo.vDebtEx d where d.asset_id = @asset_id " +
                "union " +
                "select e.lien_position, e.unlock_share_estimate, 'UNLOCK', null, null, e.unlock_share_estimate, e.effective_date from dbo.vAssetsEx e where e.asset_id = @asset_id order by d.lien_position", server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetLienTable()
        {
            DataTable tbl = new DataTable();
            tbl.Columns.Add("lien_position", typeof(int));
            
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 1 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 2 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 3 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 4 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 5 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 6 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 7 });
            tbl.Rows.Add(new object[] { 8 });

            return tbl;
        }

        public static int InsertUpdateDebt(string server, int? debt_id, string asset_id, DateTime asOf, int? lender_id, int? servicer_id, int? debttype_id, double? rate, double balance, int? lien_position, string rate_formula, DateTime? account_closed, string note, bool initial, double? payment, double? escrow_balance, double? escrow_draw_monthly, DateTime? account_open_date, DateTime? expiration_date, double? credit_limit, double? princ_payoff_amt, int? craccount_id, bool cr_reported, bool paid_off_at_origination, bool subordinated, int? subordinationtype_id)
        {

            string sql = "exec [InsertUpdateDebt] @debt_id=@debt_id, @asset_id=@asset_id, @asOf=@asOf, @lender_id=@lender_id, @servicer_id=@servicer_id, @debttype_id=@debttype_id, @balance=@balance, @rate=@rate, @lien_position=@lien_position, @rate_formula=@rate_formula, @account_closed=@account_closed, @note=@note, @initial=@initial, @payment=@payment,@escrow_balance=@escrow_balance, @escrow_draw_monthly=@escrow_draw_monthly,@account_open_date=@account_open_date,@maturity_date=@maturity_date, @credit_limit=@credit_limit, @princ_payoff_amt=@princ_payoff_amt, @craccount_id=@craccount_id, @cr_reported=@cr_reported, @paid_off_at_origination=@paid_off_at_origination, @subordinated=@subordinated, @subordinationtype_id=@subordinationtype_id, @debt_id_new=@new_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@debt_id", debt_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@lender_id", lender_id);
            q.AddParameter("@servicer_id", servicer_id);
            q.AddParameter("@debttype_id", debttype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@rate", rate);
            q.AddParameter("@balance", balance);
            q.AddParameter("@lien_position", lien_position);
            q.AddParameter("@rate_formula", rate_formula);
            q.AddParameter("@account_closed", account_closed);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@initial", initial);
            q.AddParameter("@payment", payment);

            q.AddParameter("@escrow_balance", escrow_balance);
            q.AddParameter("@escrow_draw_monthly", escrow_draw_monthly);
            q.AddParameter("@account_open_date", account_open_date);
            q.AddParameter("@maturity_date", expiration_date);
            q.AddParameter("@credit_limit", credit_limit);
            q.AddParameter("@princ_payoff_amt", princ_payoff_amt);
            q.AddParameter("@craccount_id", craccount_id);
            q.AddParameter("@cr_reported", cr_reported);
            q.AddParameter("@paid_off_at_origination", paid_off_at_origination);
            q.AddParameter("@subordinated", subordinated);
            q.AddParameter("@subordinationtype_id", subordinationtype_id);


            q.AddParameter("@new_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            int new_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@new_id"]);
            return new_id;
        }

        public static DataSet TradeLineMapping(string server, int paymentThreshold, int balanceThreshold, int openDateThreshold, bool updateMappings, List<string> includeOnlyAssets)
        {
            if (null == includeOnlyAssets)
                includeOnlyAssets = new List<string>();
            string sql = "exec dbo.TradeLineMapping @input_payment_threshold=@input_payment_threshold, @input_balance_threshold=@input_balance_threshold, @input_open_date_threshold=@input_open_date_threshold,  @updateMappings=@updateMappings, @assetsList=@assetsList";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            q.AddParameter("@input_payment_threshold", paymentThreshold);
            q.AddParameter("@input_balance_threshold", balanceThreshold);
            q.AddParameter("@input_open_date_threshold", openDateThreshold);
            q.AddParameter("@updateMappings", updateMappings);
            q.AddParameter("@assetsList", includeOnlyAssets);

            return q.Execute();
        }
    }

        public static void InsertDefaultEvent(string server, string default_id, int defaulteventtype_id, DateTime date, bool cured, DateTime? cure_date)
        {

        public static DataTable GetProtectiveAdvanceSchedule(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select d.date,-sum(a.exercise_value_cutoff+a.secured_debt) [amount] from vDefaultEventsEx d join vAssetsExCutoff a on d.asset_id = a.asset_id left join vExpensesEx e on d.asset_id = e.asset_id and e.expensetype_id=9 where d.defaulteventtype_id=5 and d.date>=dbo.TodayNY() and (e.status is null or e.status='Pending') group by d.date";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static string GetBankruptcyInfo(string server, string assetId)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(assetId))
                return string.Empty;

            try
            {
                string sql = @"
                    select top 1 cure_date
                    from vDefaultsEx
                    where default_reporting_type = 'Bankruptcy'
                      and asset_id = @asset_id
                    order by 
                        case when cure_date is null then 0 else 1 end,
                        default_date desc";

                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@asset_id", assetId);

                var dt = q.ExecuteTable();
                if (dt.Rows.Count == 0)
                    return string.Empty; 

                object cureObj = dt.Rows[0]["cure_date"];
                if (cureObj == DBNull.Value)
                    return "Active BK";

                return "Inactive BK";
            }
            catch
            {
                
            }

            return string.Empty;
        }

        public static bool GetREOInfo(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(asset_id))
                return false;

            const string sql = @"
                select case 
                         when exists (select 1 from REO where asset_id = @asset_id) 
                         then 1 else 0 
                       end as has_reo";

            try
            {
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
                int exists = q.ExecuteSingle<int>("has_reo");
                return exists == 1;
            }
            catch
            {
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BadgerLib\DocPackages.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class DockPackage
    {
     
        public struct PackageHelper
        {
            public int docconfig_id;
            public bool recorded;
            public bool executed;
        }
        public static List<PackageHelper> GetDocConfigs(string server,int docpackage_id)
        {
            string sql = "select docconfig_id,recorded,executed from vDocPackageMap dp where dp.docpackage_id = @docpackagemap_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@docpackagemap_id", docpackage_id);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            List<PackageHelper> ph = new List<PackageHelper>();
            foreach(DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                PackageHelper p = new PackageHelper();
                p.docconfig_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(row["docconfig_id"]);
                p.recorded = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["recorded"]);
                p.executed = System.Convert.ToBoolean(row["executed"]);
                ph.Add(p);
            }
            return ph;
        }
    }
}

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class Docs

        public static DataTable GetLatestDocGenDocs(string server,string state_specific)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vDocs d where d.latest = 1 and d.hide = 0 and d.docgen_enabled = 1 and ((d.state is null or @state is null) or (@state is not null and d.state = @state)) order by d.doc_name desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@state", state_specific);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int? GetAppropriateDocID(string server,string asset_id,List<int> docconfig_id)
        {
            return GetAppropriateDocIDInternal(server, server, docconfig_id, "doc_id");
        }
        public static int? GetAppropriateDocConfigID(string server, string asset_id, List<int> docconfig_id)
        {
            return GetAppropriateDocIDInternal(server, asset_id, docconfig_id, "docconfig_id");
        }

        public static int? GetAppropriateDocIDInternal(string server, string asset_id, List<int> docconfig_id,string return_field)
        {
            string sql = "select d.* from vDocs d left join vAssets a on a.state = d.state and a.asset_id = @asset_id join @docconfig_id dc on dc.item = d.docconfig_id where  (d.state is null or a.state is not null) AND D.LATEST = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@docconfig_id", docconfig_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>(return_field);
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllDocs(string server,string state)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vDocs d where (d.latest = 1 or d.latest is null) and d.hide = 0 and ((d.state is null or @state is null) or (@state is not null and d.state = @state)) order by d.doc_name asc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@state", state);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        
        

        

        public static string GenerateFilename(string server, string asset_id, int docconfig_id, string existing_filename, bool executed, bool recorded)
        {
            string file_format = BadgerLib.Docs.GetFileNameFormat(server, docconfig_id);
            Dictionary<string, object> all_vars = BadgerLib.Assets.GetAllAttributes<object>(server, asset_id);
            DateTime? created = null;
            if(!String.IsNullOrEmpty(existing_filename))
                created = File.GetCreationTime(existing_filename);

            Dictionary<string, object> final_vars = new Dictionary<string, object>();
            foreach(KeyValuePair<string,object> kvp in all_vars)
            {
                final_vars.Add($"@{kvp.Key}@", $"{kvp.Value}");
            }
            
           
            if(null != existing_filename)
                final_vars.Add("@file_create_day@", created.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd"));

            string filename = UtilsLib.Clean.CommonVariables(file_format, null, final_vars);
            if (recorded)
                filename += " - Recorded";
            else if (executed)
                filename += " - Executed";
            if(null != existing_filename)
                filename += Path.GetExtension(existing_filename);
            string directory = Path.GetPathRoot(filename);

            string filename_fixed = Clean.CleanFilename(filename, false);

            return filename_fixed;
            
        }



        public static string FigureOutFullDocName(string server,string exsisting_filename,string asset_id,int docconfig_id,bool executed,bool recorded,bool create_folder_if_no_exists)
        {
            string base_folder = BadgerLib.Docs.GetFullLocalHEIFolderWithBase(server, asset_id, docconfig_id);
            if (!Directory.Exists(base_folder))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(base_folder);

            string filename = BadgerLib.Docs.GenerateFilename(server, asset_id, docconfig_id, exsisting_filename, executed, recorded);
            string final_name = Path.Combine(base_folder, filename);
            if (create_folder_if_no_exists && !Directory.Exists(base_folder))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(base_folder);

            return final_name;
        }
        public static Dictionary<string,object> GetDocGenCommonFields(string server, string asset_id,int doc_id)
        {
            var fields = BadgerLib.Docs.GetCommonAttributes<object>(server, asset_id, true,null);
            string revision = BadgerLib.Docs.GetRev(server, doc_id);
            fields.Add("document.revision", revision);
            return fields;
        }

        public static int GetLatestDocIdFromDocConfigFromAsset(string server, int docconfig_id, string asset_id)
        {
            string state = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "state", true);
            return GetLatestDocIdFromDocConfig(server, docconfig_id, state);
        }

        public static int GetLatestDocIdFromDocConfig(string server, int docconfig_id,string state)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT d.id [doc_id] FROM DocConfig dc join Docs d on d.docconfig_id = dc.id and d.latest=1 where dc.id = @docconfig_id and (d.state is null or ISNULL(d.state,'') = ISNULl(@state,''))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@docconfig_id", docconfig_id);
            q.AddParameter("@state", state);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("doc_id");
        }


        public static string GetDocFromSharepoint(string server, int document_id,string asset_id)
        {
            string base_consumer_doc_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_CONSUMER_DOCS_LOCAL, true);

            string doc_name = BadgerLib.Docs.GetDocName(server, document_id);
            string rev_name = BadgerLib.Docs.GetRev(server, document_id);

            string state_name = BadgerLib.Docs.GetStateLabel(server, document_id);
            string doc_name_final = $"{doc_name} - {state_name} - {rev_name}";
            if(null == rev_name)
                doc_name_final = $"{doc_name} - {state_name}";

            string hei_last_name = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "last_name", true);
            string doc_name_no_ext = $"{doc_name_final} - {hei_last_name}";
            string ext = "docx";

            string full_location = $"{base_consumer_doc_location}\\{doc_name}\\{doc_name_final}.{ext}";

            string save_to = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), doc_name_no_ext + $".{ext}");

            UtilsLib.FileLib.CopySmart(full_location, save_to);
            
            return save_to;
        }
