        public static string GetFullLocalHEIFolderWithBase(string server, string asset_id, int docconfig_id)
        {
            string base_doc_folder = GetFileBaseFolder(server, docconfig_id);
            string base_homeowner_folder = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id);
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(base_doc_folder))
                return base_homeowner_folder;
            string new_folder = Path.Combine(base_homeowner_folder, base_doc_folder);
            return new_folder;
        }



        public static string ApplyVariablesToRTFHTML(string html_rtf, Dictionary<string,string> vars)
        {
            string final_answer = html_rtf;
            foreach(KeyValuePair<string,string> var in vars)
            {
                final_answer = final_answer.Replace(var.Key, var.Value);
            }
            return final_answer;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, T> GetCommonAttributes<T>(string server, string asset_id,bool do_missing,string surround_variable_with)
        {
            Query q = new Query("DocGenGeneric.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            var r = q.ExecuteDictSingleRow<T>();
            if(null != surround_variable_with)
            {
                Dictionary<string, T> new_list = new Dictionary<string, T>();
                foreach(var s in r)
                {
                    string new_key = $"{surround_variable_with}{s.Key}{surround_variable_with}";
                    new_list.Add(new_key, s.Value);
                }
                r = new_list;

            }
            if(do_missing)
            {
                List<string> blank_keys = new List<string>();
                foreach(KeyValuePair<string,T> kvp in r)
                {
                    if(typeof(T) == typeof(string))
                    {
                        if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(kvp.Value as String))
                            blank_keys.Add(kvp.Key);
                    }
                }
                foreach(string missing in blank_keys)
                {
                    
                    r.Remove(missing);
                }
            }
            return r;
        }


        public static T GetDocConfigAttribute<T>(string server, int docconfig_id, string attribute)
        {
            string sql = "select * from DocConfig d where d.id = @docconfig_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@docconfig_id", docconfig_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(attribute);
        }

        public static string GetDocCustodian(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select v.name from vAssetsEx a left join vPositionsAll p on p.asset_id = a.asset_id AND p.is_trade=0 left join vAccounts ac on ac.account_id = p.account_id left join vVendors v on v.vendor_id = ac.doccustodian_id  where(a.asset_id = @asset_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name");
        }

        public static DataTable PopualteQCExceptions(string server, DateTime begin, DateTime end,bool include_open,bool include_closed,bool corrected_only, int? monday_id, int? priority_level)
        {

            q.AddParameter("@begin", begin);
            q.AddParameter("@end", end);
            q.AddParameter("@include_open", include_open);
            q.AddParameter("@include_closed", include_closed);
            q.AddParameter("@corrected_only", corrected_only);
            q.AddParameter("@monday_id", monday_id);
            q.AddParameter("priority_level", priority_level);

            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataSet PopulateExceptions(string server, string asset_id, int? guideline_id, bool populate_table,bool show_results)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ProcessExceptions @asset_id=@asset_id, @guideline_id=@guideline_id, @populate_table=@populate_table, @show_results=@show_results";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@guideline_id", guideline_id);
            q.AddParameter("@populate_table", populate_table);
            q.AddParameter("@show_results", show_results);
            return q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetExceptionsAllInvestors(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            Query q = new Query("ExceptionsAllInvestors.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataSet GetExceptions(string server, string asset_id, int guideline_id)
        {
            DataSet set = new DataSet();
            DataTable parents = GetExceptionsInternal(server, asset_id, guideline_id, false).Copy();
            parents.TableName = "Parent";
            DataTable children = GetExceptionsInternal(server, asset_id, guideline_id, true).Copy();
            children.TableName = "Children";
            set.Tables.Add(parents);
            set.Tables.Add(children);
            set.Relations.Add(parents.Columns["exception_id"], children.Columns["parent_exceptionid"]);
            return set;
        }

        public static DataTable GetExceptionsInternal(string server, string asset_id, int guideline_id,bool only_children)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vExceptionsEx e where e.asset_id = @asset_id and e.guideline_id = @guideline_id and is_child = @only_children";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@guideline_id", guideline_id);
            q.AddParameter("@only_children", only_children);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllUsersInfo(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT user_id, first_name, last_name, email, title, departments, monday_id FROM vUsers WHERE active=1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }

        public static bool SpawnUPSAssetFolderPreBadger(string server,string asset_folder_name_only)
        {
            string local_location = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_HEI_LOCATION_OPS_LOCAL);
            string final = Path.Combine(local_location, asset_folder_name_only);
            return SpawnAssetFolderInternal(server, null, false, final);
        }


        public static bool SpawnAssetFolderInternal(string server, string asset_id, bool normalize_asset_directory,string local_location)
        {
            
            string important_file = GetFileWorksheet(server, asset_id,true);
            important_file = null;
            if (null == local_location)
            {
                
                return false;
            }
            if (normalize_asset_directory)
                NormalizeAssetDirectory(server, asset_id,true);

            if (null != important_file)
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectoryWithFileSelect(important_file, true);
            else
                UtilsLib.ProcessHelper.SpawnDirectory(local_location, true);
            return true;
        }



        
        
        
        
        
        public static string GetFileWorksheet(string server, string asset_id,bool write_if_found_or_missing)
        {
            string local_location = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id);
            string db_location = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "file_worksheet", true);
            if(null != db_location)
            {
                string full_location = Path.Combine(local_location, db_location);
                return full_location;
            }

            string found = GetFileWorksheet(local_location);
            if(write_if_found_or_missing)
            {
                string filename_only = Path.GetFileName(found);
                BadgerLib.Assets.WriteGenericAssetElement(server, "Underwriting", "file_worksheet", filename_only, "asset_id", asset_id);
            }
            return found;
        }

        }

        public static string GetImportantFileInternal(string local_location, string search,string ignores,SearchOption so = SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
        {

        public static bool NormalizeAssetDirectory(string server, string asset_id,bool cache)
        {
            if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_id))
            {
                
                return false;
            }
            string local_base_asset_folder = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id, cache);
            return NormalizeAssetDirectory(local_base_asset_folder);
        }

        public static bool NormalizeAssetDirectory(string local_base_asset_folder)
        {
            
            string fully_executed = Path.Combine(local_base_asset_folder, "Closing Docs - Fully Executed");
           

            if (!Directory.Exists(fully_executed))
                Directory.CreateDirectory(fully_executed);

            return true;
        }

        public static string GenerateUAMFolderName(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string last_name = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "last_name", true);
            string address_1 = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "address_full", true);
            string new_folder_name = $"{last_name} - {address_1}";
            return new_folder_name;
        }
        public static bool TransferToBrokerSharepoint(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string asset_folder = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id, true, true);
            
            
            string folder_name = UtilsLib.FileLib.FolderNameOnly(asset_folder);
            string state = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server,asset_id,"state",true);
            string broker_folder = Database.Common.GetGlobal(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.BASE_STATE_LICENSING_LOCATION_LOCAL, true, true);
            string full_new_location = $"{broker_folder}\\{state}\\{folder_name}";
            DateTime effective_date = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<DateTime>(server, asset_id, "effective_date", true);

            if (Directory.Exists(full_new_location))
                return false;

            UtilsLib.FileLib.CopyFullDirectory(asset_folder, full_new_location, null, false, true, effective_date);
            return false;
        }

--- FILE: BadgerLib\ForeignIDs.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class ForeignIDs
    {
        public static int ForeignIDAssociateUpdate(string server,int foreign_id,int foreignidtype_id, string asset_id, string extra,int? foreign_id_extra_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ForeignIDAssociateUpdate @asset_id=@asset_id, @foreign_id=@foreign_id, @foreignidtype_id=@foreignidtype_id, @extra=@extra, @foreign_id_extra_id=@foreign_id_extra_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@foreignidtype_id", foreignidtype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id", foreign_id);
            q.AddParameter("@extra", extra);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_id_extra_id", foreign_id_extra_id);

            int new_id = q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            return new_id;
        }



        public static string Label(string server, int foreignid_id)
        {
            return GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, foreignid_id, "label", true);
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, int foreignid_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vForeignIdsEx a where a.foreignid_id = @foreignid_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@foreignid_id", foreignid_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
            
            
        }

    }
}

            q.AddParameter("@AssetID", AssetID);

        public static int InsertUpdateInsurance(string server,string asset_id, int? insurance_id, int insurancecarrier_id, DateTime? effective_date, DateTime? policy_start_date, DateTime? policy_end_date, string policy_number, double? coverage_amount,DateTime verified_date,string note,bool? unlock_insured,double? annual_premium,int? insurancetype_id,DateTime? cancel_date)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.InsertUpdateInsurance @insurance_id = @insurance_id, @asset_id=@asset_id , @insurancecarrier_id=@insurancecarrier_id, @verified_date=@verified_date, @effective_date=@effective_date, @policy_start_date=@policy_start_date, @policy_end_date=@policy_end_date,@policy_number=@policy_number, @coverage_amount=@coverage_amount, @note=@note, @unlock_insured=@unlock_insured, @annual_premium=@annual_premium, @insurancetype_id=@insurancetype_id, @cancel_date=@cancel_date, @insurance_id_new=@new_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            
            q.AddParameter("@insurance_id", insurance_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@insurancecarrier_id", insurancecarrier_id);
            q.AddParameter("@effective_date", effective_date);
            q.AddParameter("@policy_start_date", policy_start_date);
            q.AddParameter("@policy_end_date", policy_end_date); 
            q.AddParameter("@policy_number", policy_number);
            q.AddParameter("@coverage_amount", coverage_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@verified_date", verified_date);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@unlock_insured", unlock_insured);
            q.AddParameter("@annual_premium", annual_premium);
            q.AddParameter("@insurancetype_id", insurancetype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@cancel_date", cancel_date);
            q.AddParameter("@new_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            int new_id = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@new_id"]);
            return new_id;
        }

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetIntegrityCheckTable(string server, int? priority_level)
        {
            string sql; 
             if(priority_level == null)
                sql = "select * from vIntegrityChecksEx where active = 1 order by priority_rank,integritychecktype_id,check_name";
             else
                sql = "select * from vIntegrityChecksEx where active = 1 and priority_rank <= " + priority_level.ToString() + " order by priority_rank, integritychecktype_id, check_name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Lenders.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Lenders
    {
        public static DataTable GetLenderLookupTable(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select name, id from Lenders l union select name,lender_id from LenderMap order by name";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetLegalLenderLookupTable(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select name, id, l.name_legal from Lenders l where name_legal is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }



        public static int CreateLenderIfNoExists(string server, string name)
        {
            return GetLenderId(server, true, name, null).Value;
        }

        public static Nullable<int> GetLenderId(string server, bool create_if_no_exists, string name, Nullable<int> lendertype_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetLenderId @name=@name, @create_if_no_exists=@create_if_no_exists, @lendertype_id = @lendertype_id, @lender_id=@lender_id|OUT OUTPUT";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@create_if_no_exists", create_if_no_exists);
            q.AddParameter("@lendertype_id", lendertype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@lender_id|OUT", -1);
            q.Execute();
            Nullable<int> acct = null;
            if (DBNull.Value != q.Parameters["@lender_id"])
                acct = System.Convert.ToInt32(q.Parameters["@lender_id"]);
            return acct;
        }
    }
}

        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, string asset_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select top 1 * from vLienAlertRaw a where (a.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_parse(@asset_id as decimal(18,0))) order by asOf desc";
            
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
            return t;
        }
        public static void InsertLien(string server, int load_id, string asset_id, int lender_id, int lien_position, DateTime recording_date, double amount, string loan_type, string finance_type,double? rate, DateTime? maturity_date,bool is_arm, string arm_index, double? arm_floor, double? arm_ceiling, double? arm_margin, string arm_reset_freq, double? max_int, int? io_period, double? fixed_step, DateTime? first_reset_change_date, string ppy_rider, string ppy_penalty_rider,int process_id)
        {

            string sql = @"
                            INSERT INTO dbo.Liens(
                               asset_id
                              , load_id
                              ,lender_id
                              ,lien_position
                              ,recording_date
                              ,amount
                              ,loan_type
                              ,finance_type
                              ,rate
                              ,maturity_date
                              ,is_arm
                              ,arm_index
                              ,arm_floor
                              ,arm_ceiling
                              ,arm_margin
                              ,arm_reset_freq
                              ,max_int
                              ,io_period
                              ,fixed_step
                              ,first_reset_change_date
                              ,ppy_rider
                              ,ppy_penalty_rider
                            ) VALUES (
                               @asset_id  -- asset_id - dbo.asset_id_type
                              ,@load_id
                              ,@lender_id   -- lender_id - int
                              ,@lien_position   -- lien_position - int
                              ,@recording_date -- recording_date - date
                              ,@amount
                              ,@loan_type -- varchar(45)
                              ,@finance_type -- varchar(45)
                              ,@rate -- float
                              ,@maturity_date -- date
                              ,@is_arm -- bit
                              ,@arm_index -- float
                              ,@arm_floor -- float
                              ,@arm_ceiling -- float
                              ,@arm_margin -- float
                              ,@arm_reset_freq -- varchar(45)
                              ,@max_int -- float
                              ,@io_period -- int
                              ,@fixed_step -- varchar(45)
                              ,@first_reset_change_date -- date
                              ,@ppy_rider -- varchar(45)
                              ,@ppy_penalty_rider -- varchar(45)
                            )
                            ";

            Query q = new Query(sql,server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id<varchar>", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@load_id", load_id);
            q.AddParameter("@lender_id", lender_id);
            q.AddParameter("@lien_position", lien_position);
            q.AddParameter("@recording_date", recording_date);
            q.AddParameter("@amount", amount);
            q.AddParameter("@loan_type", loan_type);
            q.AddParameter("@finance_type", finance_type);
            q.AddParameter("@rate", rate);
            q.AddParameter("@maturity_date", maturity_date);
            q.AddParameter("@is_arm", is_arm);
            q.AddParameter("@arm_index", arm_index);
            q.AddParameter("@arm_floor", arm_floor);
            q.AddParameter("@arm_ceiling", arm_ceiling);
            q.AddParameter("@arm_margin", arm_margin);
            q.AddParameter("@arm_reset_freq", arm_reset_freq);
            q.AddParameter("@max_int", max_int);
            q.AddParameter("@io_period", io_period);
            q.AddParameter("@fixed_step", fixed_step);
            q.AddParameter("@first_reset_change_date", first_reset_change_date);
            q.AddParameter("@ppy_rider", ppy_rider);

            q.AddParameterDictionary<object>(parms, null);

        public static string MaxwellDiligenceNameForAssetID(string server, string Asset_ID)
        {
            string sql = "select Diligence_Name from Maxwell_Diligence_Asset_Map where asset_id = @Asset_ID";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@Asset_ID", Asset_ID);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("Diligence_Name");
        }

        public static int MaxwellAssetCountForTradeID(string server, string Trade_ID)
        {
            string sql  = "select count(*) as asset_count from Maxwell_Diligence_Asset_Map where asset_id in (select asset_id from Trades where trade_id = @Trade_ID) ";
            Query q_SnowFlake = new Query(sql, server);
            q_SnowFlake.AddParameter("@Trade_ID", Trade_ID);
            return q_SnowFlake.ExecuteSingle<int>("asset_count");
        }

        public static void LoadAssetsIntoSample(string server, string Diligence_Name, List<string> assets)
        { 
            foreach (string asset in assets)
            {
                string sql = "insert into Maxwell_Diligence_Asset_Map (Diligence_Name, asset_id) values (@Diligence_Name, @asset_id);";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
                q.AddParameter("@Diligence_Name", Diligence_Name);
                q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset);
                q.Execute();    
            }
        }
        public static void UpdateMaxwellMasterRecord(string server, string Diligence_Name,DateTime Submitted_Date, string DiligenceDirectory, string Maxwell_Transaction_ID, int Asset_Count, string Client)
        {
            

            string sql = "exec sp_Maxwell_UpdateDiligenceMaster @Diligence_Name, @Submitted_Date, @Directory, @Maxwell_Transaction_ID, @Asset_Count, @Client";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@Diligence_Name", Diligence_Name);
            q.AddParameter("@Submitted_Date", Submitted_Date);
            q.AddParameter("@Directory", DiligenceDirectory);
            q.AddParameter("@Maxwell_Transaction_ID", Maxwell_Transaction_ID);
            q.AddParameter("@Asset_Count", Asset_Count);  
            q.AddParameter("@Client", Client);

        public static DataTable GetDocRelatedIntegrityNotes(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            
            string sql = "SELECT last_update,i.[check_name],note,priority,status,n.* FROM vNotesEx n join vForeignIds fi on fi.foreignid_id = n.foreignid_id join vIntegrityChecksEx i on i.integritycheck_id = fi.foreign_id wHERE n.asset_id = @ASSET_ID and n.note_foreignidtype_id = 3 AND (i.integritychecktype_id = 5 OR i.parentintegritychecktype_id = 5) and latest = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            return q.ExecuteTable();

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Payoffs.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class Payoffs
    {
        public static bool PayoffsExist(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            DataTable payoffs = PayoffTable(server, asset_id);
            return payoffs.Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static DataTable PayoffTable(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vPayoffs p where p.asset_id = @asset_id ORDER BY PAYOFF_NUM ASC";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


    }

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Permissions.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Permissions
    {
        private static List<Permission> _permission_list = new List<Permission>();
        public struct Permission
        {
            public string Name { get; set; }
            public int permissiontype_id { get; set; }
            public string key { get; set; }

        }

        public static bool CanRemoveAssetFromShipment { get { return HasPermission("CanRemoveAssetFromShipment"); } }

        public Permissions()
        {
        }

        public Permissions(string server)
        {
            _GetAllPermissions(server);
        }

        public static bool HasPermission(string keyvalue)
        {

            foreach (Permission permission in _permission_list)
            {
                if (permission.key == keyvalue)
                {
                    return true;
                }
            }
            return false;
        }
        private static void _GetAllPermissions(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vMyPermisisons";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            _permission_list.Clear();
            foreach (DataRow row in tbl.Rows)
            {
                Permission permission = new Permission();
                permission.Name = row["type"].ToString();
                permission.key = row["key"].ToString();
                permission.permissiontype_id = Convert.ToInt32(row["permissiontype_id"]);
                _permission_list.Add(permission);
            }
        }


        public static List<Permission> GetAllPermissions(string server)
        {
            _GetAllPermissions(server); 
            return _permission_list;
        }



    }
}

        {
            string sql = "SELECT count(*) [count],sum(p.investment_payment) [investment_payment],m.sub_stage,m.rank from vPipelineEx p join MondaySubStages m on m.sub_stage = p.sub_stage group by m.sub_stage,m.rank order by m.rank";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


        public static DataTable GetPipeline(string server, List<string> stages)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select * from vPipelineEx p join @stages s on s.item=p.sub_stage", server);
            q.AddParameter("@stages", stages);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetPendingSignature(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT asset_id,name,sub_stage,investment_payment,estimated_signing,exception FROM vPipelineEx WHERE sub_stage='Pending Signature' and pending_fund=0 ORDER BY estimated_signing";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetPendingClose(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT count(*) [#],estimated_signing,format(estimated_signing,'ddd') [day_of_week],sum(case when funding_date is null then p.investment_payment else 0 end) [not_funded],sum(case when funding_date is not null then p.investment_payment else 0 end) [already_funded], sum(p.investment_payment) [total] FROM vPipelineMaxEx p left join vAssets a on a.max_id = p.max_id where sub_stage not in ('Closed Lost','Closed Won') AND GROUP_NAME NOT IN ('Lost','Won','Paused Deals') and sub_stage in ('Pending Wire','Pending Signature','Pending Escrow Disbursement','Pending Doc Draw') group by estimated_signing ORDER BY ESTIMATED_SIGNING";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }


        public static DataTable GetPendingCloseStage(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT count(*) [#],sub_stage,sum(case when funding_date is null then p.investment_payment else 0 end) [not_funded],sum(case when funding_date is not null then p.investment_payment else 0 end) [already_funded], sum(p.investment_payment) [total] FROM vPipelineMaxEx p left join vAssets a on a.max_id = p.max_id where sub_stage not in ('Closed Lost','Closed Won') AND GROUP_NAME NOT IN ('Lost','Won','Paused Deals') and sub_stage in ('Pending Wire','Pending Signature','Pending Escrow Disbursement','Pending Doc Draw') group by sub_stage ORDER BY sub_stage";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static string NameFromAddressIgnoreDupes(string server, string address, bool use_cache)
        {
            return NameFromAddress(server, address, use_cache, new List<string>(new string[] { "Pending App Submit" }));
        }

        public static string NameFromAddress(string server, string address,bool use_cache, List<string> ignore_sub_stages)
        {
            if (null == ignore_sub_stages)
                ignore_sub_stages = new List<string>();
            address = address.Replace(" ", "%").Replace("'","''");
            string sql = $"select p.* from vPipeline p left join @ignore_sub_stages i on i.item = p.sub_stage where NAME like '%{address}%' and i.item is null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@ignore_sub_stages", ignore_sub_stages);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("name");
        }

        public static T? GetInternalAttributeFromLabel<T>(string server, string label, bool include_lost, bool ignore_dupes,string internal_field) where T : class
        {
            long? pipeline_id = GetPipelineIdFromLabel(server, label, include_lost, ignore_dupes);
            if(null != pipeline_id)
            {
                return GetAttributeInternal<T>(server, pipeline_id.Value, internal_field);
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static long? GetPipelineIdFromLabel(string server,string label,bool include_lost,bool ignore_dupes)
        {
            if (null == label)
                return null;
            label = label.Replace(" ", " ").Replace(" "," ");
            string sql = $"select * from vPipeline p where NAME = @label and (@include_lost = 1 OR (@include_lost = 0 AND group_name not in ('Lost'))) and (@ignore_dupes=0 or (@ignore_dupes=1 and p.ignore_dupes =0))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@label", label);
            q.AddParameter("@include_lost", include_lost);
            q.AddParameter("@ignore_dupes", ignore_dupes);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<long>("pipeline_id");
        }

        public static string Exception(string server,string name)
        {
            long? id = GetPipelineIdFromLabel(server, name, false, true);
            return Exception(server, id.Value);
        }

        public static string Exception(string server, long id)
        {
            return GetAttributeInternal<string>(server, id, "exception");
        }

        public static string GetPipelineLabel(string server, string asset_id)

            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);

            return q.ExecuteSingle<String>("name");
        }

        public static int AddToFundingTable(string server, DataTable dt, out List<string> assets_removed, DateTime? Value_Date = null)
        {
            assets_removed = new List<string>();
            for (int i = dt.Rows.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
            {
                DataRow dr = dt.Rows[i];
                if ((FundingExists(server, dr["ASSET_ID"].ToString())))
                {
                    assets_removed.Add(dr["ASSET_ID"].ToString());
                    dr.Delete();
                }
            }

            List<string> insert_statements = Database.DBUtils.GenerateInsertStatements("Fundings_New", dt, true, true).inserts_raw_dog;
            foreach (string insert in insert_statements)
            {
                Query q = new Query(insert, server);
                q.Execute();
            }
            return insert_statements.Count;
        }

        }

        public static string GetApplicantNameLabelFromMAX(string server, string asset_id)
        {

            string sql = "SELECT STRING_AGG(concat(FIRST_NAME, ' ',LAST_NAME), ' & ') as applicant_full_name ";
            sql += " FROM api_application app ";
            sql += " LEFT JOIN api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL ";
            sql += " LEFT JOIN api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID AND pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL ";
            sql += " WHERE app.DELETED_AT IS NULL";
            sql += " and app.EXTERNAL_ID = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);

            return q.ExecuteSingle<String>("applicant_full_name");
        }

        public static T GetAttributeInternal<T>(string server,string name,string attribute,bool ignore_dupes)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vPipeline p where name = @name and (@ignore_dupes = 0 or (p.ignore_dupes = 0 and @ignore_dupes = 1))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@name", name);
            q.AddParameter("@ignore_dupes", ignore_dupes);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(attribute);
        }

        public static T GetAttributeInternal<T>(string server, long pipeline_id, string attribute)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vPipeline where pipeline_id = @pipeline_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@pipeline_id", pipeline_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(attribute);
        }

        public static T GetAttributeInternal<T>(string server,string asset_id,string attribute)
        {
            string sql = "select p.* from vAssetsEx a join vPipelineEx p on p.pipeline_id = a.pipeline_id where a.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(attribute);
        }

        public static DataTable GetBulkFundingData(string server, bool is_summary, DateTime value_date)
        {
            Query q = new Query("BulkFunding.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@is_summary", is_summary);
            q.AddParameter("@value_date", value_date);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetTCBDrawRequestData(string server, DateTime cutoff_date, List<string> assets)
        {
            Query q = new Query("TCBDrawRequest.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutoff_date);

            DataTable results = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (null != assets && assets.Count > 0)
            {
                
                for (int i = results.Rows.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
                    if (!assets.Contains(results.Rows[i]["asset_id"].ToString()))
                        results.Rows.RemoveAt(i);
            }
            return results;
        }
    }

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class Portfolio
    {

        public static DataSet GetBalanceSheetTape(string server, DateTime cutOff)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.GetBalanceSheetTape @cutoff=@cutoff";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutOff);
            return q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataSet GetMontEndTape(string server, List<int> accounts, DateTime cutoff, List<string> only_include_assets,
    bool blankTrade, bool blankPrice, bool tradeTD, bool tradeSD, bool includeZeroPositions, bool deleteTradesIfNotReported,
    bool processExceptions, bool includeExceptions)
        {
            if (null == only_include_assets)
                only_include_assets = new List<string>();
            string sql = "exec dbo.GenerateTape_new @accounts=@accounts, @include_zero_positions=@include_zero_positions, " + "@blank_trade=@blank_trade,@blank_price=@blank_price,@trade_td=@trade_td,@trade_sd=@trade_sd,@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported=@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported," +
                "@process_exceptions=@process_exceptions,@include_exceptions=@include_exceptions, @cutoff=@cutoff ";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            q.AddParameter("@accounts", accounts);
            q.AddParameter("@include_zero_positions", includeZeroPositions);
            q.AddParameter("@blank_trade", blankTrade);
            q.AddParameter("@blank_price", blankPrice);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_td", tradeTD);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_sd", tradeSD);
            q.AddParameter("@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported", deleteTradesIfNotReported);
            q.AddParameter("@process_exceptions", processExceptions);
            q.AddParameter("@include_exceptions", includeExceptions);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutoff);

            return q.Execute();


        }

        public static DataSet GetTape(string server, List<int> accounts, DateTime cutoff, List<string> only_include_assets,
    bool blankTrade, bool blankPrice, bool tradeTD, bool tradeSD, bool includeZeroPositions, bool deleteTradesIfNotReported,
    bool processExceptions, bool includeExceptions)
        {
            if (null == only_include_assets)
                only_include_assets = new List<string>();
            string sql = "exec dbo.GenerateTape @accounts=@accounts, @cutoff=@cutoff, @only_include_assets=@only_include_assets, " + "@blank_trade=@blank_trade,@blank_price=@blank_price,@trade_td=@trade_td,@trade_sd=@trade_sd,@include_zero_positions=@include_zero_positions,@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported=@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported," +
                "@process_exceptions=@process_exceptions,@include_exceptions=@include_exceptions";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            q.AddParameter("@accounts", accounts);
            q.AddParameter("@cutoff", cutoff);
            q.AddParameter("@only_include_assets", only_include_assets);
            q.AddParameter("@blank_trade", blankTrade);
            q.AddParameter("@blank_price", blankPrice);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_td", tradeTD);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_sd", tradeSD);
            q.AddParameter("@include_zero_positions", includeZeroPositions);
            q.AddParameter("@delete_trades_even_if_not_investor_reported", deleteTradesIfNotReported);
            q.AddParameter("@process_exceptions", processExceptions);
            q.AddParameter("@include_exceptions", includeExceptions);

            return q.Execute();
        }

        public static DataTable GetFullPortfolioTable(string server,int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select  p.*,a.*,t.* from vPositions p join vAssetsEx a on a.asset_id = p.asset_Id join vTrades t on t.trade_id = p.last_trade_id and a.asset_id = t.asset_id and p.account_id = t.account_id AND t.buy_sell = 'B' where p.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetBalanceSheetPositions(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select p.account, p.investment_payment, a.asset_id, a.max_id, a.name_simple, a.address_full, a.state, n.amount [funded_amount], a.investment_pct, a.occupancy_type, a.lien_position, a.credit_score, a.ltv, a.total_home_finance, a.total_home_finance_limit, a.msa_name, a.cost_limit, a.exchange_rate, a.property_type, s.funding_status " +
                " from dbo.vPositions p " +
                " join dbo.vAssetsEx a on p.asset_id = a.asset_id " +
                " left join dbo.Fundings_New n on a.asset_id = n.asset_id and n.fundingstatus_id in (2,3) " +
                " left join dbo.FundingStatus s on n.fundingstatus_id = s.id " +
                " where (p.account in ('UPS BUYBACK','UPS') or (p.account = 'UFT1' AND n.amount is not null))" + " and a.final_disposition_date is null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static int? HistorialInvestor(string server, string asset_id, DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "select account_id,asset_id,sum(net_oface) from vTrades t where t.settle_date <= @asOf and asset_id = @asset_id group by account_id,asset_id having sum(net_oface)>0";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            if (tbl.Rows.Count == 1)
                return System.Convert.ToInt32(tbl.Rows[0]["account_id"]);
            return null;
            
        }
        public static int? GetCurrentInvestor(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vPositions p where p.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;  
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("account_id");
        }


        public static int GetLastInvestor(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT TOP 1 * FROM vTradesEx t where t.asset_id = @asset_id and buy_sell = 'B' and is_journal = 0 order by trade_date desc ";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>("account_id");
        }


        public static DataTable GetPortfolioStats(string server,List<int> account_ids)
        {
            string sql = "select account_id,account,SUM(p.remaining_investment_payment) [INVESTMENT_PAYMENT], sum(orig_buy_total_proceeds) [PURCHASE_PROCEEDS] from vPositionsAllSDCutoff p join @accts a on a.item = p.account_id where p.remaining_investment_payment != 0 group by account";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@accts", account_ids);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
               
        }
        public static List<string> GetAllPositions(string server, int account_id,bool include_paidoff)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vPositionsAll p where p.account_id = @account_id and (@include_paidoff = 1 or (@include_paidoff = 0 and remaining_investment_payment >0))";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@include_paidoff", include_paidoff);
            return q.ExecuteList<string>("asset_id");
            
        }

        public static double GetPosition(string server, DateTime asOf, int account_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT sum(t.net_oface) [inv_pmt] from vTrades t where t.settle_date <= @asOf and account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<double>("inv_pmt");

        }


        public static DataTable GetPositionStrats(string server, List<int> accts,bool include_paidoff)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT account,count(*) [count],sum(p.orig_buy_investment_payment) [invested_dollars] FROM vPositionsAll p join @accts a on a.item = p.account_Id and (@include_paidoff = 1 or (@include_paidoff = 0 and remaining_investment_payment >0)) group by account order by sum(orig_buy_investment_payment) DESC";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@accts", accts);
            q.AddParameter("@include_paidoff", include_paidoff);
            return q.ExecuteTable();

        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BadgerLib\PropertyInfo.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class PropertyInfo
    {
        public static bool PropertyInfoExists(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vPropertyinfo p where p.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static bool CountyExists(string server, string state, string county)
        {
            string sql = "select * from Counties c where c.state = @state and c.county = @county";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@state", state);
            q.AddParameter("@county", county);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }

        public static async Task<DataTable> GetCountiesByState(string server, string state)
        {
            string sql = "select county from Counties c where c.state = @state";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@state", state);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return await q.ExecuteTableTask();
        }

        public static DataTable GetCountyInfo(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            Query q = new Query("select c.state,c.county,tax_cycle,tax_website [url_2],case when tax_website is null then null else 'Link' end [url_caption_2],tax_restricted," +
                "recording_website [url_3],case when recording_website is null then null else 'Link' end [url_caption_3],rec_restricted,c.note from Counties c join vAssetsEx a on c.county = a.county AND c.state = a.state where a.asset_id = @asset_id", server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

    }
}

using static System.Windows.Forms.VisualStyles.VisualStyleElement;

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Settlements
    {
        public static DataTable GetSettlementTable(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM vSettlementsEx s where s.asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetSettlementTable(string server, DateTime start_date, string account_id)
        {
            string sql = "select s.closing_date,s.effective_date,s.unlock_share,s.asset_id,a.address_full,a.name_simple,s.settlement_type from vSettlementsEx s join vAssetsEx a on s.asset_id = a.asset_id where closing_date >= @start_date AND s.account_id = @account_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@start_date", start_date);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetFundSourceLookup(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [fundsource_id], name from FundSource";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable SettlementTypeLookup(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [settlementtype_id], name from SettlementTypes";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable SettlementReasonLookup(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [settlementreason_id], name from SettlementReasons";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable CashReceived(string server,int settlement_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vSettlementTransEx s where s.settlement_id = @settlement_id order by date asc, banktrans_id asc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@settlement_id", settlement_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable BankTransTypeLookup(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vBankTransTypes";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static bool SettlementExists(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vSettlements where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.RecordExists();
        }

        public static string GetSettlementID(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select settlement_id from vSettlements where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("settlement_id");
        }

        public static bool PartialPaymentExists(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vPartialPayments where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.RecordExists();
        }

        public static string GetPartialPaymentID(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select max(partialpayment_id) [partialpayment_id] from vPartialPayments where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<string>("partialpayment_id");
        }

        public static DataTable GetFRBCollTransactions(string server, double net_amount, double fuzzy, long? bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select frbinv_id,account_name,account_number,net_amount,file_create_date,reference_nbr,supplementary_details,tran_type,transaction_date,transaction_description from vFRBInvEx where (net_amount = @net_amount) or (net_amount between @net_amount-@fuzzy and @net_amount+@fuzzy) and (account_number=@bankacct_id)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@net_amount", net_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@fuzzy", fuzzy);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetJPMTransactions(string server, double net_amount, double fuzzy, long bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select jpminv_id,account_name,account_number,amount_cr,amount_dr,file_create_date,bank_ref,customer_ref,remark,description,asof_date,value_date from vJPMInvEx" +
                " where ((amount_cr = @net_amount) or (amount_cr between @net_amount - @fuzzy and @net_amount + @fuzzy))" +
                " or ((amount_dr = @net_amount) or (amount_dr between @net_amount - @fuzzy and @net_amount + @fuzzy))" +
                " and (account_number = @bankacct_id) order by jpminv_id desc";
                Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@net_amount", net_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@fuzzy", fuzzy);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetTCBTransactions(string server, double net_amount, double fuzzy, long bankacct_id)
        {
            string sql = "select tcbinv_id,asofdate,acctno,acctname,trandesc,debitamt,creditamt,customerrefno,desctext,companyidentification,transactiontype,file_create_date from vTCBInvEx" +
                " where ((creditamt = @net_amount) or (creditamt between @net_amount - @fuzzy and @net_amount + @fuzzy))" +
                " or ((debitamt = @net_amount) or (debitamt between @net_amount - @fuzzy and @net_amount + @fuzzy))" +
                " and (acctno = @bankacct_id) order by tcbinv_id desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@net_amount", net_amount);
            q.AddParameter("@fuzzy", fuzzy);
            q.AddParameter("@bankacct_id", bankacct_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetMonthlySettlements(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select  EOMONTH(s.closing_date) [month], sum(s.settlement_costs) [amt], count(*) [terminations] " +
                "from dbo.Settlements s " +
                "where s.closing_date >= GetDate() - 90 " +
                "group by EOMONTH(s.closing_date) " +
                "order by EOMONTH(s.closing_date) desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static DataTable GetSettlementRequest(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select asset_id,statement_date,settlement_type,ending_home_value,settlement_reason,improvement_adjustment, maintenance_adjustment, credits, other_expenses from vSettlementRequestsEx where asset_id=@asset_id and latest=1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetPartialPayments(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select value_date,account_name,payoff_amount,starting_factor,starting_investment_payment,ending_factor,ending_investment_payment,unlock_share,note from vPartialPaymentsEx where asset_id = @asset_id order by value_date asc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static DataTable GetZenSettlementRequests(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select ASSET_ID, TICKET_TYPE, AVM_VALUE, CREATED_AT, UPDATE_TIME, ZENTICKET_ID, SUBJECT from ZenSettlementRequests where ASSET_ID = @asset_id order by UPDATE_TIME desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static bool HasActiveSettlementRequest(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(asset_id))
                return false;

            string sql =
                "SELECT * FROM vSettlementRequests " +
                "WHERE asset_id = @asset_id " +
                "  AND statement_void_after >= GETDATE()";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.RecordExists();
        }

        public static DataTable GetIncomingSettlementWires(string server, bool processedOnly)
        {
            string sql = @"SELECT * FROM vIncomingSettlementWires WHERE PROCESSED = @Processed";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@Processed", processedOnly);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }
}

select 
  a.applicant_id
  , ae.applicanttype_id
  , ae.applicant_type
  , a.first_name
  , a.middle_name
  , a.last_name
  , a.suffix
  , a.email
  , a.phone
  , a.dob
  , ssn
  , a.mailing_address_full
  , a.maritalstatus_id
  , a.primary_address_1
  , a.primary_address_2
  , a.primary_city
  , a.primary_state
  , a.primary_zip

  , a.mailing_address_1
  , a.mailing_address_2
  , a.mailing_city
  , a.mailing_state
  , a.mailing_zip
  , a.full_name
  
  , a.date_of_death
  , ae.deceased
  from 
    vApplicantsEx ae
    join vApplicants a on a.applicant_id = ae.applicant_id
    
  where
    ae.asset_id = @asset_id


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\AssetsOnBs.sql ---
select

sum(a.investment_payment) [inv_pmt]
from
  vClosingEx c
  join vAssets a on a.asset_id = c.asset_id
  left join vTradesGOS_UAH_AND_BUYBACK_AS_CPY t on t.asset_id = c.asset_id
where
  c.funding_date is not null
  and (t.settle_date > @settle_date or t.settle_date is null)
  and c.funding_date <= @settle_date
  and (t.account_id = @account_id or t.account_id is null)


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\BatchCreditReport.sql ---
SELECT 
distinct
 replace(replace(a1.first_name,'.',''),'’','') [BorFirstName]
, REPLACE(a1.middle_name,'.','') [BorMiddleName]
, replace(REPLACE(a1.last_name,'.',''),',','') [BorLastName]
, a1.suffix [BorSuffix]
, a1.ssn [BorSSN]
, a1.dob [BorDOB]
, replace(replace(a2.first_name,'.',''),'’','') [CoBorFirstName]
, REPLACE(a2.middle_name,'.','') [CoBorMiddleName]
, replace(REPLACE(a2.last_name,'.',''),',','') [CoBorLastName]
, a2.suffix [CoBorSuffix]
, a2.ssn [CoBorSSN]
, a2.dob [CoBorDOB]
, isnull(a1.primary_address_1,pri.address_simple) [StreetAddress]
, isnull(a1.primary_city,pri.city) [City]
, isnull(a1.primary_state,pri.state) [State]
, isnull(a1.primary_zip,pri.zip) [ZipCode]
, null PrevStreetAddress
, null PrevCity
, null PrevState
, null PrevZipCode

, pri.address_full PropertyAddress
, convert(varchar(30),a1.applicant_id) + case when a2.applicant_id is not null then '|' + convert(varchar(30),a2.applicant_id) else '' end [RefNumber]
, null [LoanType]
, a.phone_formatted [Phone]
, a.email [Email]
, 'NO' XPcredit
, 'YES' TUcredit
, 'NO' EFcredit
, 'NO' XPscore
, 'YES' TUscore
, 'NO' EFscore
, 'NO' XPfraud
, 'NO' TUfraud





  FROM
    vAssetsEx a
    join vApplicants a1 on a1.applicant_id = a.applicant_id
    join vAssetApplicantPrimaryHome vaph on a1.applicant_id = vaph.applicant_id
    left join vApplicants a2 on a2.applicant_id = a.applicant_co_id
    left join vAssetsEx pri on pri.asset_id = vaph.asset_id
    
  where
    a.final_disposition_date is null
    
    and a.effective_date <= eomonth(dateadd(m,-1,GetDate()),0)
    
    
    
  order by
    replace(REPLACE(a1.last_name,'.',''),',','')


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\BulkFunding.sql ---
DROP table IF exists #tmp



	
SELECT APP.EXTERNAL_ID, STRING_AGG(concat(FIRST_NAME, ' ',LAST_NAME), ' & ') [full_name]
INTO #tmp FROM API_APPLICATION APP
LEFT JOIN api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
LEFT JOIN api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID AND pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL
WHERE convert(varchar(50),app.EXTERNAL_ID) IN (SELECT asset_id FROM Fundings_New WHERE fundingstatus_id=1 AND value_date=@value_date)
GROUP BY APP.EXTERNAL_ID;

IF (@is_summary=1)
BEGIN
SELECT 
    COUNT(*) AS Num_of_Assets, 
    SUM(c.investment_payment) AS Sum_of_Inv_Payments,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 9 THEN 1 END) AS CET_Num_of_Assets,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 48 AND c.[State] = 'HI' THEN 1 END) AS FAHI_Num_of_Assets,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 48 AND c.[State] <> 'HI' THEN 1 END) AS FA_Num_of_Assets,
    SUM(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 9 THEN c.investment_payment ELSE 0 END) AS CET_Sum_of_Inv_Payments,
    SUM(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 48 AND c.[State] = 'HI' THEN c.investment_payment ELSE 0 END) AS FAHI_Sum_of_Inv_Payments,
    SUM(CASE WHEN f.titleescrowcompany_id = 48 AND c.[State] <> 'HI' THEN c.investment_payment ELSE 0 END) AS FA_Sum_of_Inv_Payments
FROM vClosingEx c 
JOIN Fundings_New f ON c.asset_id = f.asset_id 
WHERE f.fundingstatus_id = 1 AND f.value_date = @value_date;
END
ELSE BEGIN
  
WITH expenses AS
(  
 SELECT APP.external_id,CASE WHEN dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to)='Accurategroup' THEN 'Accurate Group' ELSE dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to) END AS [appraisal_vendor],exp.amount [appraisal_fee],ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY APP.external_id ORDER BY exp.amount) AS RowNumber
 FROM API_APPLICATION APP
 LEFT JOIN api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
 LEFT JOIN api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID AND pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 LEFT JOIN API_EXPENSE exp on exp.application_id = app.id AND exp.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 WHERE exp.[name] LIKE 'Appraisal%' and convert(varchar(50),app.EXTERNAL_ID) IN (SELECT asset_id FROM Fundings_New WHERE fundingstatus_id=1 AND value_date=@value_date)
 GROUP BY APP.external_id, dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to),exp.amount
),
concessions AS
(
SELECT 
	APP.external_id
	
	,exp.amount [concessions]
	,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY APP.external_id ORDER BY exp.amount) AS RowNumber
 FROM API_APPLICATION APP
 LEFT JOIN api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
 LEFT JOIN api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID AND pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 LEFT JOIN API_EXPENSE exp on exp.application_id = app.id AND exp.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 WHERE exp.[name] LIKE 'Concession%' and convert(varchar(50),app.EXTERNAL_ID) IN (SELECT asset_id FROM Fundings_New WHERE fundingstatus_id=1 AND value_date=@value_date)
 GROUP BY APP.external_id, dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to),exp.amount 
)
SELECT DISTINCT
c.asset_id
,dbo.ProperCase(p.address) as [Homeowner Address]
,c.investment_payment
,expense1.appraisal_fee + ISNULL(expense2.appraisal_fee,0) as [Appraisal Fee Amount]
,orig_expense.amount as [Origination Fee]
,c.net_wire_amt as [Total Wire Amount]
,c.file_num as [File Number]
,#tmp.full_name [Property Owner(s)]
,con.concessions
,f.title_escrow_company
,CASE WHEN c.[State]='HI' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS is_HI
FROM vClosingEx c
JOIN vPipeline p on p.asset_id=c.asset_id
JOIN #tmp on c.asset_id=CONVERT(varchar(50),#tmp.EXTERNAL_ID)
LEFT JOIN expenses as expense1 on c.asset_id=CONVERT(varchar(50),expense1.EXTERNAL_ID) and expense1.RowNumber=1
LEFT JOIN expenses as expense2 on c.asset_id=CONVERT(varchar(50),expense2.EXTERNAL_ID) and expense2.RowNumber>1 and expense2.appraisal_fee!=795  
LEFT JOIN (select distinct application_id,amount from API_EXPENSE expense where expense."TYPE" ='origination_charge') orig_expense on p.application_id=orig_expense.APPLICATION_ID
LEFT JOIN concessions con on con.external_id = c.asset_id
JOIN vFundings_New f on c.asset_id = f.asset_id 
WHERE f.fundingstatus_id = 1 AND f.value_date =@value_date

END;

drop table #tmp


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\BulkFundingFaster.sql ---
WITH expenses AS
(  
 SELECT APP.external_id,
	CASE 
		WHEN dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to)='Accurategroup' THEN 'Accurate Group' 
		ELSE dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to) 
		END AS [appraisal_vendor],
		exp.amount [appraisal_fee],
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY APP.external_id ORDER BY exp.amount) AS RowNumber
 FROM API_APPLICATION APP
 LEFT JOIN api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
 LEFT JOIN api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID AND pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 LEFT JOIN API_EXPENSE exp on exp.application_id = app.id AND exp.DELETED_AT IS NULL
 WHERE exp.[name] LIKE 'Appraisal%' and convert(varchar(50),app.EXTERNAL_ID) IN (SELECT asset_id FROM Fundings_New WHERE  value_date=@value_date)
 GROUP BY APP.external_id, dbo.ProperCase(exp.paid_to),exp.amount
)
select 
	c.asset_id,
	RIGHT(c.customer_pipeline_label, CHARINDEX('-', REVERSE(c.customer_pipeline_label)) - 1) as [Homeowner Address],
	c.investment_payment,
	
	expense1.appraisal_fee + ISNULL(expense2.appraisal_fee,0) as [Appraisal Fee Amount],
	c.origination_fee [Origination Fee],
	c.net_wire_amt [Total Wire Amount],
	c.file_num [File Number],
	c.Concession [concessions],
	REVERSE(SUBSTRING(REVERSE(c.customer_pipeline_label), 
                         CHARINDEX('-', REVERSE(c.customer_pipeline_label)) + 1, 
                         LEN(c.customer_pipeline_label)))  as [Property Owner(s)],
	f.title_escrow_company,
	case a.state
		when 'HI' THEN 1
		else 0
	end [is_HI]
from Closing c
JOIN vFundings_New f on c.asset_id = f.asset_id 
left join assets a on a.id = c.asset_id
LEFT JOIN expenses as expense1 on c.asset_id=CONVERT(varchar(50),expense1.EXTERNAL_ID) and expense1.RowNumber=1
LEFT JOIN expenses as expense2 on c.asset_id=CONVERT(varchar(50),expense2.EXTERNAL_ID) and expense2.RowNumber>1 and expense2.appraisal_fee!=795  
WHERE  f.value_date =@value_date;


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CapAmounts.sql ---
select 
  d.date
  , dbo.CapAmount(a.cost_limit_basis,a.cost_limit,a.effective_date,d.date) [cap_amount]
  from 
    vAssets a
    cross join Dates d
  where
    d.last_day_month_calendar = 1
    and d.date <= a.expiration_date
    and d.date >= a.effective_date
    and a.asset_id = @asset_id
  order by
    d.date desc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CollatShipmentSummary.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp
drop table if exists #count

declare @stage varchar(150)
select @stage=[value] FROM Globals g where g.[key] = 'DOC_CUSTODIAN_STAGE'

SELECT

  cs.collatshipment_id
  , cs.asof
  , cs.collatshiptype_id
  , cs.nice_name
  , cs.ship_date
  , cs.shipped
  , cs.tracking_number
  , cs.doccustodian_id
  , cst.[type] [ship_type]
  
  
  , @stage+'\' + cs.staging_folder + '\' [staging_folder]
  , REPLACE(SUBSTRING(
        (
            SELECT ', '+a.name_simple  AS [text()]
            FROM vAssetsEx a
            left join (select distinct collatshipment_id, asset_id from dbo.CollatshipmentMap ) csm on csm.collatshipment_id = cs.collatshipment_id
            WHERE a.asset_id = csm.asset_id
            ORDER BY a.name_simple
            FOR XML PATH ('')
        ), 2, 1000), '&amp;','&') [assets]
        , dbo.GetTrackingUrl(cs.tracking_number) [url]
        , case when cs.tracking_number is null then null else 'Track' end [url_caption]
         
        
        
  into #tmp
  FROM 
    vCollatShipments cs
    left join CollatShipmentTypes cst on cs.collatshiptype_id = cst.id
    left join CollatshipmentMap csm on csm.collatshipment_id = cs.collatshipment_id
    left join Docs d on d.id = csm.doc_id
    left join DocConfig dc on dc.id = d.docconfig_id
    
    
    
    
  WHERE (cs.shipped = 0 and @show_all=0) or (@show_all=1)

  order by
    asOf desc
   

  
  select c.collatshipment_id,count(distinct c.asset_id) [#] into #count from vCollatShipmentMap c  join #tmp t on t.collatshipment_id = c.collatshipment_id group by c.collatshipment_id
  
  select distinct
   isnull(c.[#],0) [#]
   ,t.collatshipment_id
  , asof
  , collatshiptype_id
  , nice_name
  , ship_date
  , shipped
  , tracking_number  
  , case when collatshiptype_id = 1 then 'Open Folder' else 'Track' end url_caption
  , case when collatshiptype_id = 1 then staging_folder else url end [url]
  , format(asof,'M/d') + ' - ' + ship_type + CASE WHEN nice_name is not null then ' - ' + nice_name else '' end + case when assets is null then '' else ' - ' + assets end [ship_label] 
  , format(asof,'M/d') + ' - ' + ship_type + CASE WHEN nice_name is not null then ' - ' + nice_name else '' end + ' - ' + convert(varchar(20),isnull(c.[#],0)) + ' HEIs'[ship_label_short] 
  , staging_folder
  , doccustodian_id
  from 
    #tmp t
    left join #count c on c.collatshipment_id = t.collatshipment_id
    order by asOf desc
    
  drop table #tmp
  drop table #count


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CostlyTrades.sql ---
drop table if exists #market
drop table if exists #tmp

select 
  ticket_id
  , trade_id
  , account
  , buy_sell
  , counterparty
  , asset_id
  , name_simple
  , address_simple
  , investment_payment
  , price
  , dirty_price
  , premium_recapture
  , uam_fee
  , other_fees
  , market_value
  , trade_date
  , settle_date 
  , case when is_buyback = 1 then investment_payment else null end BUYBACK_INV_PMT
  , case when IS_SCRATCH_DENT = 1 then (106.00-PRICE)/100.00*INVESTMENT_PAYMENT else null end SCRATCH_DENT
  , CASE WHEN is_buyback = 1 then 'BUYBACK' when IS_SCRATCH_DENT=1 THEN 'SCRATCH & DENT' WHEN HAS_PREMIUM_RECAPTURE =1 THEN 'PREMIUM RECAPTURE' END [TYPE]
  , t.is_buyback
  , t.is_scratch_dent
  , t.has_premium_recapture
  into #tmp
  from 
    vTradesEx t 
  where 
    t.buy_sell = 'B'
    and (t.is_unlock = 0) and (t.counterparty_is_unlock = 1 or t.is_buyback = 1)
    AND
    ((@include_buybacks=1 and is_buyback = 1 ) or (@include_scratch_dent =1 and is_scratch_dent = 1) or (@include_premium_recaptures=1 and has_premium_recapture=1))
  
  SELECT trade_id,sum(t.price*t.oface)/sum(t.oface) [wavg_price], count(*) [#] into #market FROM vTrades t group by trade_id
  
  update t set [TYPE] = 'MARKET MOVEMENT' from #tmp t join #market m on m.trade_id = t.trade_id where [TYPE] = 'SCRATCH & DENT' and wavg_price not between 105.5 and 106.5 and [#] > 10
    
  select * from #tmp
  
    
 drop table #tmp
 drop table #market


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CreditScores.sql ---
SELECT 
  cs.asof
  , cs.creditfile_id
  , cs.full_name
  , cs.bureau
  , cs.credit_score
  , cs.initial
  , cs.latest
  , cs.vendor_id
  , cs.applicant_id
  , cs.creditscoremodel_id
  , cs.creditscore_id
  , cs.load_id
  , cs.model_type
  from
  vCreditScores cs
  join AssetApplicantMap aam on cs.applicant_id = aam.applicant_id
  where
    aam.asset_id = @asset_id
  order by
    cs.asOf desc
    , cs.model_type
    , cs.full_name
    , cs.bureau


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CRSNeededOrders.sql ---
select 
  a.asset_id 
    from vAssets a 
    join vUnderwriting u on u.asset_id = a.asset_id 
    
    left join CRQueue q on q.applicant_id = a.applicant_id and isnull(q.applicant_co_id,0) = isnull(a.applicant_co_id,0) and q.requesttype_id = 2
    where 
      a.final_disposition_date is null 
      and u.[4506_filename] is not null 
      and a.effective_date > '2/13/2023'
      AND q.applicant_id IS NULL
