--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\CustomerPipelineNew.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp
drop table if exists #ship


declare @days_to_ic int = 2



drop table if exists #ship
drop table if exists #close
    
select 
  max(ship_date) [ship_date]
  , max(ship_date) [ship_date_effective]
  , asset_id 
  into #ship
  from 
    vCollatShipmentDetailEx 
  where 
    collatshiptype_id = 1 
  group by asset_id


    
select 
p.asset_id
, p.investment_payment
, cast(s.ship_date as date) [ship_date]
, a.effective_date
, s.ship_date_effective
, convert(bit,0) [certified]
, convert(date,null) [projected_ic_date]
, convert(date,null) [next_trade_date]
, convert(date,null) [next_settle_date]
, convert(varchar(200),null) [customer_pipeline_label]
, convert(varchar(200),null) [sub_stage]
, convert(date,null) [estimated_signing]
into #tmp
  from 
    vPositions p
    left join #ship s on s.asset_id = p.asset_id
    join vAssets a on a.asset_id = p.asset_id
  where 
    p.account_id = 1
    and a.final_disposition_date is null
    
    
    

alter table #tmp alter column effective_date date null

insert into #tmp (asset_id,customer_pipeline_label,sub_stage,investment_payment,estimated_signing,effective_date) select asset_id, p.[name] ,sub_stage,investment_payment,estimated_signing,effective_date from vPipelineEx p where p.sub_stage = 'Pending Signature' and p.group_name = 'Active Pipeline' and p.asset_id not in (select asset_id from #tmp t)



update t set certified = 1 from #tmp t join vAvailableCollateral c on c.asset_id = t.asset_id

update #tmp set ship_date_effective = estimated_signing where ship_date is null
update #tmp set ship_date_effective = estimated_signing where ship_date_effective is null
update #tmp set ship_date_effective = cast(dbo.GetDateNY() as date) where ship_date_effective < dbo.GetDateNY() or ship_date_effective is null


update #tmp set projected_ic_date = null where certified = 1
update #tmp set projected_ic_date = dbo.AddBDays(ship_date,@days_to_ic) where certified = 0

update #tmp set next_trade_date = DATEADD(DAY, (DATEDIFF(DAY, @trade_date, ship_date_effective) / 7) * 7 + 7, @trade_date)
update #tmp set next_settle_date = DATEADD(DAY, (DATEDIFF(DAY, @settle_date, next_trade_date) / 7) * 7 + 7, @settle_date)




select t.asset_id,isnull(t.customer_pipeline_label,c.customer_pipeline_label) [customer_pipeline_label],isnull(t.sub_stage,c.sub_stage) [sub_stage],isnull(t.investment_payment,c.investment_payment) [investment_payment],isnull(t.estimated_signing,c.estimated_signing) [estimated_signing],null [funding_date],ship_date,ship_date_effective,projected_ic_date,isnull(funded,0) [funded],isnull(originated,0) [originated],net_wire_amt,sign_eta_orig,next_trade_date,next_settle_date,disbursement_eta,convert(date,null) [disbursement_effective],c.note into #close from #tmp t left join vClosingEx c on c.asset_id = t.asset_id

update c set disbursement_effective = case when disbursement_eta is null then ship_date_effective else disbursement_eta end from #close c 

select * from #close 

drop table if exists #tmp
drop table if exists #ship
drop table if exists #close


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\DailyAvailableToTrade.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmpFunding
drop table if exists #tmpFundingPivot
drop table if exists #tmpFundingSummary

select 
  b.nice_name [funded account],
  ac.*, 
  n.funding_status [unlock_funding_status], 
  n.value_date, 
  case 
    when ac.WSFS_Certification_Status = 'Certified' and ac.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 1 then 'TRUE'
    else 'FALSE'
    end [available to trade]
into #tmpFunding
from dbo.vAvailableCollateral ac
  left outer join dbo.vFundings_New n on ac.asset_id = n.asset_id and n.funding_status != 'Cancelled' and n.funding_type = 'Deal'
  left outer join dbo.BankAccts b on b.id = n.bankacct_id
order by [available to trade] desc, ac.effective_date asc

select 
    format(getdate(),'MM/dd/yyy') [Date]
    , count(*) [# Balance Sheet]
    ,format(sum(t.investment_payment),'c','en-US') [$ Balance Sheet ]
    , sum(case when [available to trade] = 'TRUE' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) [# Tradeable]
    ,format(sum(case when [available to trade] = 'TRUE' THEN t.investment_payment ELSE 0 END),'c','en-US') [$ Tradeable]
    into #tmpFundingSummary
from #tmpFunding t



select 
    4 [order]
    ,convert(varchar(50),'Total') [Asset Status]    
    ,count(*) [#]
    ,format(sum(t.investment_payment),'c','en-US') [$]
into #tmpFundingPivot
from #tmpFunding t



insert into #tmpFundingPivot
select 
    0 [order]
    ,'Tradeable' [Asset Status]  
    ,sum(case when [available to trade] = 'TRUE' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) [Count]
    ,format(sum(case when [available to trade] = 'TRUE' THEN t.investment_payment ELSE 0 END),'c','en-US') [$]
from #tmpFunding t



insert into #tmpFundingPivot
select 
    1
    ,'Certified, not Funded'
    ,sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status = 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 0 then 1 else 0 end) [#]
    ,format(sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status = 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 0 then t.investment_payment else 0 end),'c','en-US') [$]
from #tmpFunding t



insert into #tmpFundingPivot
select 
    2,
    'Funded, not Certified'
    ,sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status <> 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 1 then 1 else 0 end) [#]
    ,format(sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status <> 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 1 then t.investment_payment else 0 end),'c','en-US') [$]
 from #tmpFunding t



insert into #tmpFundingPivot
select 
    3,
    'Not Certified or Funded'
    ,sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status <> 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 0 then 1 else 0 end) [#]
    ,format(sum(case when t.WSFS_Certification_Status <> 'Certified' and t.funds_disbursed_by_title_company = 0 then t.investment_payment else 0 end),'c','en-US') [$]
from #tmpFunding t





select CONCAT('[', t.date, ']  ', t.[$ Tradeable],' Tradeable Assets')
from #tmpFundingSummary t


select *
from #tmpFundingSummary t

select [Asset Status],[#],[$] from #tmpFundingPivot order by [order]

select * from #tmpFunding







drop table if exists #tmpFunding
drop table if exists #tmpFundingPivot
drop table if exists #tmpFundingSummary


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\DocGenGeneric.sql ---
SELECT 
  a.asset_id [agreement_id]
  , a.asset_id
  , a.apn [property_apn]
  , upper(a.title_held_in) [title_held_in]
  , upper(a.name_simple) [name_simple]
  , a.name_simple [name_nice]
  , upper(a.legal_name_all) [homeowner_names]
  , upper(a.legal_name_all) [legal_name_all]
  , format(dbo.TodayNY(),'yyyy-MM-dd') [today_yyyy-MM-dd]
  , upper(replace(t.trustee_name,'{{COUNTY}}',a.county)) [title_company_trustee]
  , upper(a.county) [property_county]
  , upper(a.state) [property_state]
  , upper(s.state_full) [property_state_full]
  , a.legal_desc [legal_description]
  , a.legal_desc [legal_desc]
  , UPPER(format(a.effective_date,'MMMM')) [asset_sale_month]
  , datepart(day,a.effective_date) [asset_sale_day]
  , datepart(year,a.effective_date) [asset_sale_year]
  , datepart(year,GetDate()) [today_year]
  , a.last_name
  , UPPER(format(a.effective_date,'M/d/yyyy')) [effective_date]
  , UPPER(format(a.effective_date,'MMMM d, yyyy')) [effective_date_long]
  , a.address_full
  , ISNULL(a.legal_desc_short,A.LEGAL_DESC) [legal_desc_short]
  , a.investment_pct [investment_pct_%]
  , a.unlock_pct [unlock_pct_%]
  , a.exchange_rate
  , a.origination_fee [origination_fee_$]
  , a.cost_limit [cost_limit_%]
  , a.doc_maintenance_addendum
  , a.doc_consent_of_spouse
  , a.starting_home_value [starting_home_value_$]
  , a.total_home_finance_limit [total_home_finance_limit_%]
  , a.investment_payment [investment_payment_$]
  , upper(dbo.SpellNumber(a.investment_payment)) [investment_payment_spelled]

  , format(a.investment_payment,'$#,##0.00') [investment_payment_formatted]
  , dbo.TodayNY() [today]
  , format(dbo.TodayNY(),'MMMM d, yyyy') [today_long]
  , format(a.buyout_active_date,'MMMM d, yyyy') [buyout_date_long]
  , upper(s.originator) [unlock_originating_entity_state]
  , a.apn
  , UPPER(format(r.close_date,'M/d/yyyy'))  [refi_close_date]
  , UPPER(format(r.close_date,'MMMM d, yyyy'))  [refi_close_date_long]
  , UPPER(r.name_legal_if_available) [refi_lender_legal]
  , r.loan_num [refi_loan_num]
  , r.rate [refi_rate]
  , format(r.rate,'0.000%') [refi_rate_formatted]
  , r.term [refi_term]
  , r.term/12 [refi_term_years]
  , upper(dbo.SpellNumber(r.term/12.0)) [refi_term_years_spelled]
  , upper(dbo.SpellNumber(r.rate*100) + ' and ' + dbo.SpellNumber((r.rate*100-convert(int,r.rate*100))*1000) + ' percent') [refi_rate_pct_spelled]
  , r.amount [refi_amount]
  , '$' + format(r.amount,'#,##0.00') [refi_amt_formatted]
  , upper(dbo.SpellNumber(r.amount)) [refi_amt_spelled]
  
  , UPPER(format(r.si_record_date_hack,'MMMM d, yyyy')) [si_record_long]
  , UPPER(format(r.si_record_date_hack,'MMMM')) [si_record_month]
  , datepart(year,r.si_record_date_hack) [si_record_year]
  , datepart(day,r.si_record_date_hack) [si_record_day]
  , r.si_record_num_hack [si_record_num]
  , a.title_vesting
  , case when u.uam_commentary is null then 'No deal commentary provided' else u.uam_commentary end [uam_commentary]
  , case when u.uam_comp_factors is null then 'No compensating factors provided' else u.uam_comp_factors end [uam_comp_factors]
  , case when u.uam_comp_factors_descr is null then 'No compensating factors description provided' else u.uam_comp_factors_descr end [uam_comp_factors_descr]
  , a.max_id
  FROM 
    vAssetsEx a
    join States s on a.state = s.state
    left join vClosing c on c.asset_id = a.asset_id
    left join vTrustees t on t.trustee_id = c.trustee_ID
    left join vRefisEx r on r.asset_id = a.asset_id and r.latest = 1
    left join vUnderwriting u on u.asset_id = a.asset_id    
  WHERE
    a.asset_id = @asset_id


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\ExceptionsAllInvestors.sql ---
SELECT 
  convert(bit,case when p.asset_id is not null then 1 else 0 end) [owns]
  , a.[name] [account]
  , e.guideline_label
  , e.exception_type
  , e.exception_desc
  , e.bounds_low
  , e.bounds_high
  , e.value_dbl
  , e.value_str
  , e.bounds_allowed_list_str
  , case when p.asset_id is not null then 'LawnGreen' else null end [row_color]
FROM 
  vAssetExceptionsEx e 
  join vAccounts a on a.account_id = e.account_id 
  left join vPositions p on p.asset_id = e.asset_id and p.account_id = a.account_id
  where 
    e.asset_id = @asset_id and latest_guideline_id =1
  order by convert(bit,case when p.asset_id is not null then 1 else 0 end) desc, ACCOUNT


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Funding_Bank_Manual_Recon.sql ---
declare @v_Amount float
set @v_Amount = convert(float, @p_Amount )

select b.id as transaction_id
	, recon.category
	, bt.transaction_type
	, transaction_date
	, b.account_id
	, amount
	, description
	, supplementary_details
from BankActivity b
left join BankActivityTransactionTypes bt on bt.id = b.transaction_type_id 
left join FundingBankReconMap recon on b.id = recon.transaction_id 
where transaction_type_id in (2) 
and transaction_date between @p_Funding_date  and DATEADD(WEEKDAY, 5, @p_Funding_date ) 
and b.account_id =  1309823 and recon.category is null 
and amount between @v_Amount -0.5 and @v_Amount +0.5 
order by transaction_date desc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Funding_Bank_Manual_Recon_Add_Mapping.sql ---
declare @p_transaction_id int
declare @p_account_id int
declare @p_update_by varchar(255)
*/

insert into FundingBankReconMap (asset_id, category, transaction_id, account_id, update_by, update_time)
values (@p_asset_id, @p_category, @p_transaction_id, @p_account_id, @p_update_by, dbo.TodayNY())


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Funding_Bank_Recon_Detail.sql ---
declare @v_sdate datetime, @v_edate datetime

select @v_sdate =min(value_date), @v_edate = max(value_date) from Fundings_New 

if isdate(@p_Funding_date) = 1
	begin
	set @v_sdate =@p_Funding_date
	set @v_edate =@p_Funding_date
	end


drop table if exists #tmp


select 
	fund.value_date as Funding_Date
	, cl.asset_id
	, cl.file_num
	, cl.investment_payment 
	, fund.fundingstatus_id
	, cl.customer_pipeline_label
	, cl.origination_fee
	, cl.pre_paid_fees
	, cl.concession as concession
	, 0 as origination_fee_bank_trans
	, 0 as pre_paid_fees_bank_trans
	, 0 as adjustment_bank_trans
	, 0 as total_fees_bank_trans
	, convert(float,0.0) as unlock_amount
	, convert(float,0.0) as bank_amount
into #tmp
from Fundings_New fund
left join FundingStatus fund_stat on fund_stat.id = fund.fundingstatus_id 
left join Closing cl on cl.asset_id = fund.asset_id 
where (fund.asset_id = @p_asset_id)
or (fund.value_date between @v_sdate and @v_edate and @p_asset_id is null)


update #tmp set origination_fee_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'origination_fee'
update #tmp set pre_paid_fees_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'pre_paid_fees'
update #tmp set total_fees_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'total_fees'
update #tmp set adjustment_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'adjustment'

update #tmp set unlock_amount = isnull(cl.origination_fee,0)+isnull(cl.pre_paid_fees,0)+isnull(cl.concession,0) from Closing cl where cl.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id update #tmp set unlock_amount = 0 where unlock_amount = 4 update #tmp set bank_amount = (select sum(bank.amount) from BankActivity bank where bank.id in (#tmp.origination_fee_bank_trans, #tmp.pre_paid_fees_bank_trans, #tmp.total_fees_bank_trans, #tmp.adjustment_bank_trans))

select Funding_Date
	, asset_id

	, investment_payment
	, fs.funding_status 
	, customer_pipeline_label
	, origination_fee
	, pre_paid_fees

	, origination_fee_bank_trans
	, pre_paid_fees_bank_trans
	, adjustment_bank_trans
	, total_fees_bank_trans
	, unlock_amount
	, bank_amount
	, (unlock_amount - bank_amount) as diff
from #tmp
left join FundingStatus fs on fs.id = #tmp.fundingstatus_id
order by fs.funding_status, customer_pipeline_label


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Funding_Bank_Recon_Summary.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp

select 
	fund.value_date as Funding_Date
	, cl.asset_id
	, cl.customer_pipeline_label
	, cl.investment_payment
	, cl.origination_fee
	, cl.pre_paid_fees
	, 0 as origination_fee_bank_trans
	, 0 as pre_paid_fees_bank_trans
	, 0 as adjustment_bank_trans
	, 0 as total_fees_bank_trans
	, fund.fundingstatus_id 
	, convert(float,0.0) as unlock_amount
	, convert(float,0.0) as bank_amount
into #tmp
from vFundings_New fund 
left join Closing cl on cl.asset_id = fund.asset_id
where fund.value_date >='10/10/2023'  

update #tmp set origination_fee_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'origination_fee'
update #tmp set pre_paid_fees_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'pre_paid_fees'
update #tmp set total_fees_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'total_fees'
update #tmp set adjustment_bank_trans = transaction_id from FundingBankReconMap recon where recon.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and recon.category = 'adjustment'


update #tmp set unlock_amount = isnull(cl.origination_fee,0)+isnull(cl.pre_paid_fees,0) from Closing cl where cl.asset_id = #tmp.asset_id and #tmp.fundingstatus_id <> 4
update #tmp set bank_amount = (select sum(bank.amount) from BankActivity bank where bank.id in (#tmp.origination_fee_bank_trans, #tmp.pre_paid_fees_bank_trans, #tmp.total_fees_bank_trans, #tmp.adjustment_bank_trans))

select Funding_Date
	, count(*) as Asset_Count
	, sum(investment_payment) as Investment_Payment
	, sum(unlock_amount) as UnLock_Amount
	, sum(bank_amount) as Bank_Amount
	, round(sum(unlock_amount) - sum(bank_amount),2) as Diff
from #tmp
group by Funding_Date
order by Funding_Date desc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Funding_Bank_Recon_Trans_Detail.sql ---
select convert(date, bank.transaction_date) as transaction_date
	, bank.account_id
	, bank.transaction_type_id
	, bat.transaction_type
	, bank.amount
	, bank.description
	, bank.supplementary_details
	, bank.note
from fundingbankreconmap recon
left join bankactivity bank on recon.transaction_id = bank.id
left join BankActivityTransactionTypes bat on bat.id = bank.transaction_type_id
where recon.asset_id = @p_asset_id

--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\MaxwellDilgenceMaster.sql ---
select mdf.diligence_name,mdf.maxwell_transaction_id, mdf.asset_count, mdf.Submitted_Date
	, count(*) as 'All'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade ='A' then 1 else 0 end)) as 'A_Count'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='B' then 1 else 0 end)) as 'B_Count'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='C' then 1 else 0 end)) as 'C_Count'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='D' then 1 else 0 end)) as 'D_Count'
	, sum((case when (overall_final_loan_grade<> 'A' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'B' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'C' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'D') then 1 else 0 end)) as 'Other_Count'
	, sum(assets.investment_payment) as 'Total_Inv_Pmt'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade ='A' then 1 else 0 end)*assets.investment_payment) as 'A_Inv_Pmt'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='B' then 1 else 0 end)*assets.investment_payment) as 'B_Inv_Pmt'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='C' then 1 else 0 end)*assets.investment_payment) as 'C_Inv_Pmt'
	, sum((case when overall_final_loan_grade='D' then 1 else 0 end)*assets.investment_payment) as 'D_Inv_Pmt'
	, sum((case when (overall_final_loan_grade<> 'A' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'B' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'C' 
				  and overall_final_loan_grade<> 'D') then 1 else 0 end)*assets.investment_payment) as 'Other_Inv_Pmt'
from Maxwell_Diligence_Master mdf
left join vMaxwellGrades grades on mdf.diligence_name= grades.diligence_name
left join vassets assets on grades.asset_id = assets.asset_id
group by mdf.diligence_name, mdf.asset_count, maxwell_transaction_id, mdf.Submitted_Date
order by mdf.Submitted_Date asc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\MaxwellDiligenceFindingDetail.sql ---
select asset_id, investment_payment, overall_final_loan_grade, finding_status, event_level, 
current_final_finding_grade, finding_category, finding_sub_category, finding_name
from vMaxwellFindings mf
where diligence_name = @diligence_name
and load_id = (select max(load_id) from vMaxwellFindings where asset_id  = mf.asset_id)
and overall_final_loan_grade not in ('A', 'B')
and current_final_finding_grade not in ('A', 'B')

--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Max_API_Table_Status_SnowFlake.sql ---
SELECT 'API_ADDRESS' AS TABLENAME, count(*) AS ROW_COUNT, DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)) AS MODIFIED_AT_DATE, TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) AS MODIFIED_AT_TIME  FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_ADDRESS
union all SELECT 'API_Application', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)) , TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_Application
union all SELECT 'API_APPLICATION_CREDIT_REPORTS', count(*), NULL, null FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATION_CREDIT_REPORTS
union all SELECT 'API_APPLICATIONEXCEPTION', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATIONEXCEPTION
union all SELECT 'API_APPLICATIONPARTY', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATIONPARTY
union all SELECT 'API_APPLICATIONPROFILE', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATIONPROFILE
union all SELECT 'API_APPLICATIONPROFILE_CREDIT_REPORTS', count(*), NULL, null FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_APPLICATIONPROFILE_CREDIT_REPORTS
union all SELECT 'API_ASSET', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_ASSET
union all SELECT 'API_CreditReport', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_CreditReport
union all SELECT 'API_DEALTEAM', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_DEALTEAM
union all SELECT 'API_Expense', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_Expense WHERE IE_ISSUE_DATE >= '1/1/2019' or IE_ISSUE_DATE is null AND DELETED_AT IS NULL AND AMOUNT <> 0
union all SELECT 'API_HOI', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_HOI
union all SELECT 'API_INCOME', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_INCOME
union all SELECT 'API_OFFER', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_OFFER
union all SELECT 'api_overrides', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.api_overrides
union all SELECT 'API_PARTY', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_PARTY
union all SELECT 'API_PROFILE', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_PROFILE
union all SELECT 'API_Property', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_Property WHERE AQUIRED_ON >= '1/1/1902' or AQUIRED_ON is NULL
union all SELECT 'API_TITLEREPORT', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_TITLEREPORT
union all SELECT 'API_TRADELINE', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_TRADELINE
union all SELECT 'API_USEOFPROCEEDS', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_USEOFPROCEEDS
union all SELECT 'API_USERINCOME', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_USERINCOME
union all SELECT 'API_VALUATION', count(*), DATE(max(MODIFIED_AT)), TIME(max(MODIFIED_AT)) FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.API_VALUATION

union all SELECT 'AUTH_USER', count(*), NULL, null FROM RAW.fivetran_max_app_prod_public.AUTH_USER;


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\MonthlyValuations.sql ---
declare @cutoff date
declare @include_paid_off bit = 1










select @cutoff = [value] from Globals g where g.[key] = 'CUTOFF'

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #tmp
drop table if exists #closeouts

select
  A.EFFECTIVE_DATE
  , a.max_id [ASSET_ID]
  , a.last_name
  , a.name_simple
  , ADDRESS_FULL
  , A.STARTING_HOME_VALUE
  , A.INVESTMENT_PAYMENT
  , A.INVESTMENT_PCT
  , A.EXCHANGE_RATE
  , A.UNLOCK_PCT
  , A.COST_LIMIT
  , A.TERM
  , A.COST_LIMIT_BASIS
  , final_disposition_date_cutoff
  , ABS(T.NET_PROCEEDS) [NET_PROCEEDS]
  , s.cash_to_remit_to_coll_calc
  , lockout_months
  , a.updated_home_value_waterfall_cutoff
  , a.unlock_share_waterfall_cutoff [exercise_value]
  , a.updated_home_value_waterfall_cutoff*a.unlock_pct [max_exercise_value]
  , t.trade_date
  , t.settle_date
  , t.ticket_id
  , a.max_id
  , t.price/100.0 [price]
  , a.cutoff_date
  , hpi_adjusted_home_value_cutoff
  , a.updated_pct_of_orig_waterfall_cutoff
into #tmp
  from
    vTrades t
    join vAssetsExCutoff a on a.asset_Id = t.asset_Id
    left join vBasePricing b on b.asset_id = a.asset_id and b.account_id = t.account_id
    left join vAccounts act on act.account_id = t.account_id
    join @accts accts on accts.item = t.account_id
    left join vTrades p on p.account_id = t.account_id and p.buy_sell = 'S' and p.asset_id = t.asset_id and p.is_journal = 1
    
    left join vSettlementsEx s on s.asset_id = a.asset_id
  where
   
    t.buy_sell = 'B'
    and t.settle_date <= @cutoff
    
    

  ORDER BY
    t.trade_id, a.name_simple
    
    
  select
    EFFECTIVE_DATE
  , ASSET_ID
  , last_name
  , ADDRESS_FULL
  , STARTING_HOME_VALUE
  , INVESTMENT_PAYMENT
  , INVESTMENT_PCT
  , EXCHANGE_RATE
  , UNLOCK_PCT
  , COST_LIMIT
  , TERM
  , COST_LIMIT_BASIS
  , lockout_months
  , updated_home_value_waterfall_cutoff
  , exercise_value
  , max_exercise_value
  , price
  , net_proceeds
  , cutoff_date
  , hpi_adjusted_home_value_cutoff
  , settle_date
  ,  UPDATED_PCT_OF_ORIG_WATERFALL_CUTOFF
  from 
    #tmp 
  where 
    final_disposition_date_cutoff is null order by effective_date asc


create table #closeouts
(
  asset_id varchar(30)
  , INVESTMENT_PAYMENT float
  , name_simple varchar(100)
  , [date] date
  , amount float
)

insert into #closeouts
  select
  ASSET_ID
  , INVESTMENT_PAYMENT
  , NAME_SIMPLE
  , EFFECTIVE_DATE
  , -net_proceeds

  from 
    #tmp   
  where
    final_disposition_date_cutoff is not null
 insert into #closeouts
  select
  ASSET_ID
  , INVESTMENT_PAYMENT
  , NAME_SIMPLE
  , final_disposition_date_cutoff
  , cash_to_remit_to_coll_calc
  from 
    #tmp   
  where
    final_disposition_date_cutoff is not null
    
  select asset_id, INVESTMENT_PAYMENT, name_simple,[date] [1],amount [0] from #closeouts  order by date asc

SELECT asset_id from #tmp where final_disposition_date_cutoff is null order by effective_date asc


select 
  s.max_id
  , s.asset_id
  , a.name_simple
  , a.address_full
  , s.closing_date
  , t.date
  , t.net_amount
  , t.note
  from 
    vSettlementsEx s
    left join vSettlementTransEx t on t.asset_id = s.asset_id and t.account_id = s.account_id
    join vAssetsEx a on a.asset_id = s.asset_id
    join @accts accts on accts.item = s.account_id
  where
    s.closing_date between @begin_coll and @end_coll





  



DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #active_assets
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #tmp
drop table if exists #closeouts


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\PipelineAddToClosing.sql ---
SELECT 
	  app.EXTERNAL_ID as asset_id
	, app.name
	, APPLICATION_STATE
	, APPLICATION_STATE_MODIFIED_AT
	, convert(date,ESTIMATED_CLOSE_ON) as ESTIMATED_CLOSE
	, (case when closing.asset_id is null then 'No' else 'Yes' end) as In_Closing_Table
	, count(expense_pre_paid_fees.NAME) as pre_paid_fees_count
	, sum(expense_pre_paid_fees.AMOUNT) as pre_paid_fees_gross
	, -1*expense_concession.AMOUNT as concession_amount
	, offer.THF_LIMIT as THF_LIMIT
	, offer.ANNUALIZED_COST_LIMIT as COST_LIMIT
	, offer.INVESTMENT_AMOUNT as investment_payment
	, app_exceptions.exception as exception
	, concat(referral.EMAIL, ' ', referral.ADDRESS, ' ', referral.CONTACT_NAME) as referral_info

FROM api_application app 
	left join vAPI_APPLICATIONEXCEPTION app_exceptions on app.EXTERNAL_ID = app_exceptions.asset_id
	left join vClosing closing on convert(varchar(255),app.EXTERNAL_ID) = closing.asset_id 
	left join api_applicationprofile app_pro ON app.ID =app_pro.APPLICATION_ID and app_pro.POSITION = 1 AND app_pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
	left join api_profile pro ON app_pro.PROFILE_ID = pro.ID and pro.DELETED_AT IS NULL
	left join vAPI_OFFER offer on offer.APPLICATION_ID = app_pro.APPLICATION_ID and offer.DELETED_AT is null
	left join API_APPLICATIONPARTY ap on ap.application_id = app.id  AND APPLICATION_PARTY_TYPE = 'party'
	left join api_party  as referral on ap.party_id = referral.id AND referral.DELETED_AT IS NULL 
	left join api_expense expense_origination ON (convert(bigint,app.id) = expense_origination .application_id and expense_origination ."TYPE" ='origination_charge')
	left join api_expense expense_pre_paid_fees on expense_pre_paid_fees.APPLICATION_ID = app.id and expense_pre_paid_fees.deleted_at is null 
	left join api_expense expense_concession on expense_concession.APPLICATION_ID = app.id and expense_concession.deleted_at is null and expense_concession.name = 'Concession' 
	join ClosingExpenseMap on expense_pre_paid_fees.name= ClosingExpenseMap.MaxExpenseName
WHERE ClosingExpenseMap.IsPrePaidExpense =1 
and APPLICATION_STATE in ('pending-signature', 'pending-escrow-disbursement')
and closing.asset_id is null
group by 
	  app.EXTERNAL_ID
	, app.name
	, APPLICATION_STATE
	, APPLICATION_STATE_MODIFIED_AT
	, ESTIMATED_CLOSE_ON
	, closing.asset_id
	, expense_concession.AMOUNT 
	, offer.THF_LIMIT 
	, offer.ANNUALIZED_COST_LIMIT 
	, offer.INVESTMENT_AMOUNT 
	, expense_origination.amount
	, offer.INVESTMENT_AMOUNT
	, app_exceptions.exception 
	, referral.EMAIL
	, referral.ADDRESS
	, referral.CONTACT_NAME


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\QualityChecklistExceptions.sql ---
if @begin is null
  set @begin = '1/1/2000'

if @end is null
  set @end= dbo.TodayNY()
  
if(@priority_level IS NULL)
begin
   select @priority_level  = 4
end

SELECT
  a.asset_id
  , a.name_simple
  , a.address_simple
  , a.address_full
  , a.investment_payment
  , c.integritycheck_id
  , c.check_name [issue_name]
  , n.status
  , n.note [last_note]
  , n.corrected
  , n.last_update
  , a.effective_date
  , c.priorityname_alt
  , c.priority_rank
  , p.last_name [processor_last_name]
  , s.last_name [sales_last_name]
  , u.last_name [underwriter_last_name]
  , cl.processor_id
  , cl.sales_id
  , cl.underwriter_id
  , n.is_open
  , c.qc_integritycheck_id
  FROM 
    vNotesEx n
    join vForeignIDs f ON n.foreignid_id = f.foreignid_id
    join vAssetsEx a on a.asset_id = n.asset_id
    join vIntegrityChecksEx c on c.integritycheck_id = f.foreign_id
    join vClosingEx cl on cl.asset_id = a.asset_id
    left join vUsers p on cl.processor_id = p.monday_id
    left join vUsers s on cl.sales_id = s.monday_id
    left join vUsers u on cl.underwriter_id = u.monday_id
  where
    
    f.foreignidtype_id = 2
    and latest = 1
    and ((a.effective_date between @begin and @end) or (n.last_update between @begin and @end))
    and ((@corrected_only is null or @corrected_only=0) or (@corrected_only =1 and n.corrected = 1))
    and c.priority_rank <= @priority_level
    and 
    (
      (@include_closed is null or (@include_closed =1 and n.is_open=0))
      or 
      (@include_open is null or (@include_open =1 and n.is_open=1))
    )
    AND
    (@monday_id is null OR @monday_id = p.monday_id OR @monday_id = s.monday_id OR @monday_id = u.monday_id)
    order by 
      c.priority_rank asc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\RollRate.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp

declare @last_credit date
select @last_credit =max(asOf) from vCreditLoads where filename like '%.csv'

if @begin is null
  set @begin = '1/1/2000'

if @end is null
  set @end= dbo.TodayNY()
  
select
  a.asset_id
  , a.name_simple
  , left(c.paystring_full,1) [status_current]
  , substring(c.paystring_full,2,1) [status_previous]
  , c.paystring_full [paystring]
  , c.date_reported
  , c.status
  , c.asOf
  , c.is_open
  , a.effective_date
  , a.investment_payment
  , d.lender_name
  , c.creditor
  , d.balance_calc
  , a.total_home_finance_limit
  , a.total_home_finance
  , a.credit_score
  , a.credit_score_calc_current
  , a.lien_position
  , a.state
  , a.starting_home_value
  , a.final_disposition_date
  , c.craccount_id
into #tmp from vDebtEx d
    join vAssetsEx a on a.asset_id = d.asset_id
    join vCRTradelinesEx c on d.craccount_id = c.craccount_id and c.asset_id = a.asset_id
    where a.effective_date <= dateadd(d,-2,@last_credit)
    and d.cr_reported = 1 and d.cr_visible=1
    and d.balance_calc > 0
    and len(c.paystring_full) >= 2
if @option=0 
(
select * from #tmp
where final_disposition_date is null
    and is_open=1
    and asOf = @last_credit
)
else if @option=1 
(
select * from #tmp
where (final_disposition_date is null or final_disposition_date > @end)
    and (asof between @begin and @end)
    and (@acct_status=0 or (@acct_status=1 and is_open=1) or (@acct_status=2 and is_open=0))
)
else if @option=2 
(
select * from #tmp
where (final_disposition_date is null or final_disposition_date > @end)
    and (@acct_status=0 or (@acct_status=1 and is_open=1) or (@acct_status=2 and is_open=0))
    and DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(asOf,-1)) = DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(@begin,-1))
    and craccount_id in (select distinct craccount_id from #tmp 
    where (final_disposition_date is null or final_disposition_date > @end)
    and (@acct_status=0 or (@acct_status=1 and is_open=1) or (@acct_status=2 and is_open=0))
    and DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(asOf,-1)) = DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(@end,-1)))
)
else if @option=3 
(
select * from #tmp
where (final_disposition_date is null or final_disposition_date > @end)
    and (@acct_status=0 or (@acct_status=1 and is_open=1) or (@acct_status=2 and is_open=0))
    and DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(asOf,-1)) = DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(@end,-1))
    and craccount_id in (select distinct craccount_id from #tmp 
    where (final_disposition_date is null or final_disposition_date > @end)
    and (@acct_status=0 or (@acct_status=1 and is_open=1) or (@acct_status=2 and is_open=0))
    and DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(asOf,-1)) = DATEADD(DAY,1,EOMONTH(@begin,-1)))
)

drop table #tmp


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\TCBDrawRequest.sql ---
BEGIN TRANSACTION

DECLARE @orig_cutoff as date
SELECT @orig_cutoff = g.[value] FROM Globals g WHERE g.[key] = 'CUTOFF'

UPDATE Globals SET [value] = CONVERT(varchar,@cutoff,101) WHERE [key] = 'CUTOFF'

    SELECT
      a.max_id [max_id]
      , a.asset_id [asset_id]
      , a.effective_date
      , a.city
      , a.zip
      , a.state
      , a.county
      , a.investment_payment_orig [investment_payment_original]
      , a.investment_pct
      , a.exchange_rate
      , a.unlock_pct
      , a.total_home_finance
      , a.total_home_finance_limit
      , a.credit_score [credit_score_origination]
      , a.cost_limit
      , a.cost_limit_basis
      , a.lien_position
      , a.property_type
      , a.occupancy_type
      , a.term
      , a.secured_debt
      , a.ltv
      , a.investment_pct+a.ltv [cltv]
      , a.property_condition
      , a.dscr
      , case when a.has_open_negam_io_mtg=0 then 'FALSE' else 'TRUE' end [negam_or_io_mtg]
      , a.dti
      , a.starting_home_value
      , a.proceeds_use
      , a.unlock_share_waterfall_cutoff [exercise_value]
      , a.updated_home_value_waterfall_cutoff*a.unlock_pct [max_exercise_value]
      , v.valuation_used [property_appraisal_type]
      , v.valuation_date [property_appraisal_date]
      , g.[value] [cutoff_date]
      , case when a.valuation_eligibility='AVM_ONLY' then 'TRUE' else 'FALSE' end [AVM_ONLY]
      , v.avm1_value
      , v.avm2_value
      , v.avm_fsd_confidence_1
      , v.avm_fsd_confidence_2
      , v.pcr_int_property_condition [pcr_property_condition]
FROM vAssetsExCutoff a
JOIN Globals g on g.[key] = 'CUTOFF'
LEFT JOIN vValuationsMax_New v on v.asset_id = a.asset_id
WHERE a.effective_date>'9/1/2024' 

     
  UPDATE Globals SET [value] = CONVERT(varchar,@orig_cutoff,101) WHERE [key] = 'CUTOFF'
  COMMIT TRANSACTION


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\TradelinePicker.sql ---
select l.is_open,l.creditor,l.date_opened,l.date_last_activity,l.high_credit_or_limit,l.balance [balance_latest],c.id [craccount_id],l.status
  from 
    CRAccounts c 
  join vCRTradelinesEx l on l.craccount_id = c.id and (l.acct_type in ('Mortgage') or l.credit_loan_type in ('Secured','HomeEquityLineOfCredit','HomeEquity','ConventionalRealEstateMortgage','CreditLineSecured')) and l.latest = 1
  
  where    
    l.asset_id = @asset_id
  order by is_open desc,l.balance desc


--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\UnpaidOwnerObligations.sql ---
drop table if exists #tmp;

WITH expenses AS ( SELECT e.asset_id,e.[type],e.[date],e.amount,ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY e.asset_id ORDER BY e.[date],e.amount) AS RowNumber FROM vExpensesEx e WHERE e.unpaid_owner_obligation=1 GROUP BY e.asset_id,e.[date],e.amount,e.[type])
SELECT asset_id
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 1 THEN [type] END [expense_type_1] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 1 THEN [date] END [expense_date_1] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 1 THEN amount END [expense_amount_1]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 2 THEN [type] END [expense_type_2] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 2 THEN [date] END [expense_date_2] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 2 THEN amount END [expense_amount_2]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 3 THEN [type] END [expense_type_3] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 3 THEN [date] END [expense_date_3] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 3 THEN amount END [expense_amount_3]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 4 THEN [type] END [expense_type_4] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 4 THEN [date] END [expense_date_4] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 4 THEN amount END [expense_amount_4]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 5 THEN [type] END [expense_type_5]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 6 THEN [type] END [expense_type_6]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 6 THEN amount END [expense_amount_6]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 7 THEN [date] END [expense_date_7]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 10 THEN [type] END [expense_type_10] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 10 THEN [date] END [expense_date_10]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 11 THEN [date] END [expense_date_11] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 11 THEN amount END [expense_amount_11]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 12 THEN [type] END [expense_type_12] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 12 THEN [date] END [expense_date_12] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 12 THEN amount END [expense_amount_12]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 13 THEN [type] END [expense_type_13] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 13 THEN [date] END [expense_date_13]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 14 THEN [type] END [expense_type_14] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 14 THEN [date] END [expense_date_14] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 14 THEN amount END [expense_amount_14]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 15 THEN [type] END [expense_type_15] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 15 THEN [date] END [expense_date_15] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 15 THEN amount END [expense_amount_15]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 16 THEN [type] END [expense_type_16] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 16 THEN [date] END [expense_date_16] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 16 THEN amount END [expense_amount_16]
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 17 THEN [type] END [expense_type_17] 
, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 17 THEN [date] END [expense_date_17]

, CASE WHEN expenses.RowNumber= 18 THEN [type] END [expense_type_18]

INTO #tmp FROM expenses
SELECT MAX(expense_type_1) [expense_type_1], MAX(expense_date_1) [expense_date_1], MAX(expense_amount_1) [expense_amount_1],

       MAX(expense_type_8) [expense_type_8], MAX(expense_date_8) [expense_date_8], MAX(expense_amount_8) [expense_amount_8],
       MAX(expense_type_9) [expense_type_9], MAX(expense_date_9) [expense_date_9], MAX(expense_amount_9) [expense_amount_9],
       MAX(expense_type_10) [expense_type_10], MAX(expense_date_10) [expense_date_10], MAX(expense_amount_10) [expense_amount_10],
       MAX(expense_type_11) [expense_type_11], MAX(expense_date_11) [expense_date_11], MAX(expense_amount_11) [expense_amount_11],
       MAX(expense_type_12) [expense_type_12], MAX(expense_date_12) [expense_date_12], MAX(expense_amount_12) [expense_amount_12],
       MAX(expense_type_13) [expense_type_13], MAX(expense_date_13) [expense_date_13], MAX(expense_amount_13) [expense_amount_13],
       MAX(expense_type_14) [expense_type_14], MAX(expense_date_14) [expense_date_14], MAX(expense_amount_14) [expense_amount_14],
       MAX(expense_type_15) [expense_type_15], MAX(expense_date_15) [expense_date_15], MAX(expense_amount_15) [expense_amount_15],
       MAX(expense_type_16) [expense_type_16], MAX(expense_date_16) [expense_date_16], MAX(expense_amount_16) [expense_amount_16],
       MAX(expense_type_17) [expense_type_17], MAX(expense_date_17) [expense_date_17], MAX(expense_amount_17) [expense_amount_17],
       MAX(expense_type_18) [expense_type_18], MAX(expense_date_18) [expense_date_18], MAX(expense_amount_18) [expense_amount_18],
       MAX(expense_type_19) [expense_type_19], MAX(expense_date_19) [expense_date_19], MAX(expense_amount_19) [expense_amount_19],
       MAX(expense_type_20) [expense_type_20], MAX(expense_date_20) [expense_date_20], MAX(expense_amount_20) [expense_amount_20]
FROM #tmp WHERE asset_id=@asset_id
GROUP BY asset_id

--- FILE: BadgerLib\SQL\Watchlist.sql ---
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #TMP
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #MTG
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #AUTO
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_latest
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_initial
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_3mo
drop table if exists #dupe
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_chg

select
  pos.account
  , l.asset_id
  , a.name_simple
  , a.investment_payment
  
  , a.age
  , l.asof [latest_asof]
  , p.asof [prior_asof]
  
  , i.credit_score_calc [credit_score_origination]
  , l.credit_score_calc [credit_score_latest]
  , p.credit_score_calc [credit_score_3mo]
  , p.asof [lookback_credit_asof]
  , l.credit_score_calc-p.credit_score_calc [credit_score_3mo_delta]
  , l.credit_score_calc-i.credit_score_calc [credit_score_life_delta]
  , convert(varchar(300),null) [mtg_status]
  , convert(varchar(300),null) [auto_status]
  
  , a.total_home_finance
  , a.secured_debt
  , a.starting_home_value
  , a.ltv
  , a.lien_position
  , a.hpi_index_calc
  , CONVERT(date,null) [watchlist_date]
  , CONVERT(int,null) [days_on_watchlist]
  , convert(varchar(40),null) [trg]
  , ini.creditfile_id [creditfile_id_initial_api] 
  , p.creditfile_id [creditfile_id_3mo]
  , i.creditfile_id [creditfile_id_initial]
  , l.creditfile_id [creditfile_id_latest]
  
  , CONVERT(FLOAT,NULL) [collection_debt_initial]
  , CONVERT(FLOAT,NULL) [collection_debt_3mo]
  , convert(float,null) [collection_debt_latest]
  
  , CONVERT(FLOAT,NULL) [collection_debt_chg_initial]
  , CONVERT(FLOAT,NULL) [collection_debt_chg_3mo]
  , convert(varchar(360),null) [uam_comments]
    , (l.credit_score_calc-i.credit_score_calc)/i.credit_score_calc [credit_score_life_pct_delta]
INTO #TMP
  from 
    vAssetsEx a
    join vCreditScoreAsset l on a.asset_id = l.asset_id
    join vCreditScoreAsset p on p.asset_id = l.asset_id and datediff(m,p.asOf,l.asOf) = @MONTHS_BACK 
    left join vCreditScoreAsset i on p.asset_id = i.asset_id and i.initial = 1
    left join vCreditScoreAsset ini on a.asset_id = ini.asset_id and ini.creditfile_id is not null
    join vCreditFiles cf on cf.creditfile_id = ini.creditfile_id and cf.initial_api = 1
    join vPositionsTDCutoff pos on a.asset_id = pos.asset_id
    join @accts accts on accts.item = pos.account_id
  where
    l.latest = 1
    
    ORDER BY (l.credit_score_calc-p.credit_score_calc) ASC


    
SELECT c.creditfile_id, string_agg(isnull(status,''),', ') [mtg_status] into #mtg FROM vCRTradelines c join #tmp t on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_latest where c.acct_type in ('Mortgage') and c.open_close = 'Open' and status not in ('AsAgreed') AND C.BALANCE > 0 group by c.creditfile_id
SELECT c.creditfile_id, string_agg(isnull(status,''),', ') [auto_status] into #auto FROM vCRTradelines c join #tmp t on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_latest where c.credit_loan_type in ('AutoLease','Automobile') AND C.BALANCE > 0 and c.open_close = 'Open' and status not in ('AsAgreed') group by c.creditfile_id


SELECT c.creditfile_id, sum(balance)[collection_debt_initial] into #coll_initial FROM vCRTradelines c join #tmp t on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_initial_api where (CREDIT_BUSINESS_TYPE = 'CollectionServices' or status in ('CollectionOrChargeOff','ForeclosureOrRepossession'))  AND C.BALANCE > 0 group by c.creditfile_id 
SELECT c.creditfile_id, sum(balance)[collection_debt_latest] into #coll_latest FROM vCRTradelines c join #tmp t on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_latest where (CREDIT_BUSINESS_TYPE = 'CollectionServices' or status in ('CollectionOrChargeOff','ForeclosureOrRepossession'))  AND C.BALANCE > 0 group by c.creditfile_id 
SELECT c.creditfile_id, sum(balance)[collection_debt_3MO] into #coll_3mo FROM vCRTradelines c join #tmp t on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_3mo where (CREDIT_BUSINESS_TYPE = 'CollectionServices' or status in ('CollectionOrChargeOff','ForeclosureOrRepossession')) AND C.BALANCE > 0 group by c.creditfile_id 



UPDATE T SET collection_debt_initial=C.collection_debt_initial FROM #TMP T join #coll_initial c on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_initial_api
UPDATE T SET collection_debt_latest=C.collection_debt_latest FROM #TMP T join #coll_latest c on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_LATEST
UPDATE T SET collection_debt_3mo=C.collection_debt_3MO FROM #TMP T join #coll_3mo c on c.creditfile_id = t.creditfile_id_3MO
UPDATE T SET collection_debt_chg_3mo=collection_debt_latest-collection_debt_3MO FROM #TMP T 
UPDATE T SET collection_debt_chg_initial=collection_debt_latest-collection_debt_initial FROM #TMP T 

update t set mtg_status = m.mtg_status from #tmp t join #mtg m on t.creditfile_id_latest = m.creditfile_id
update t set auto_status = m.auto_status from #tmp t join #auto m on t.creditfile_id_latest = m.creditfile_id





update t set trg = case when trg is null then 'MTG DLQ' else trg+' + MTG DLQ' END from #tmp t where mtg_status IS NOT NULL
update t set trg = case when trg is null then 'AUTO DLQ' else trg+' + AUTO DLQ' END from #tmp t where auto_status IS NOT NULL
update t set trg = case when trg is null then 'COLLECTION' else trg+' + COLLECTION' END from #tmp t where collection_debt_chg_initial > @coll_thresh
update t set trg = case when trg is null then 'FICO' else trg+' + FICO' END from #tmp t where credit_score_life_pct_delta < -@THRESHOLD_PCT 

update t set trg = 'WATCHLIST',uam_comments = w.uam_comments,watchlist_date = w.create_date, days_on_watchlist = datediff(d,w.create_date,dbo.GetDateNY()) from #tmp t join vWatchlistEx w on w.asset_id = t.asset_id and w.active = 1









delete from #tmp where trg is null

select count(*) [num],asset_id,max(lookback_credit_asof) latest_lookback into #dupes from #tmp group by asset_id
delete t from #tmp t join #dupes d on (d.num = 2 and d.asset_id = t.asset_id) and t.lookback_credit_asof != d.latest_lookback



delete from #tmp where mtg_status = 'Late30Days' and auto_status is null and isnull(collection_debt_chg_initial,0) < @coll_thresh and credit_score_life_pct_delta > -@THRESHOLD_PCT 
select * from #tmp order by days_on_watchlist ASC,mtg_status desc,auto_status desc,credit_score_life_pct_delta asc,trg

DROP TABLE #TMP
drop table #mtg
drop table #auto
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_latest
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_initial
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS #coll_3mo
drop table #dupes

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Surveillance.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Surveillance
    {


        public static DataTable GetRawLAData(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT top 500 l.asOf ,lo.* from LAOUT lo left join LALoads l on lo.load_id = l.id  where lo.REF_ID = @asset_id order by asOf desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            var table = q.ExecuteTable();
            table.TableName = "LA Out Raw";
            return table;
        }

        public static string GetLatestLAReport(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string folder = GetLienAlertLocalFolder(server, asset_id);
            var directory = new DirectoryInfo(folder);
            var file = directory.GetFiles().OrderByDescending(f => f.LastWriteTime).First();
            return file.FullName;
        }
        public static string GetLienAlertLocalFolder(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string asset_folder = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, asset_id);
            string asset_LienAlert_folder = Path.Combine(asset_folder, "LienAlert");
            return asset_LienAlert_folder;
        }
       
    }
}


--- FILE: BadgerLib\Tasks.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Tasks
    {
        public static void ResetTasks(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.ResetAllTasks @asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.Execute();
        }

        public static bool TaskSetExistsOnAsset(string server,string asset_id,int taskset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select count(*) from vTasks t where t.taskset_id = @taskset_id and t.asset_id=@asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@taskset_id", taskset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable().Rows.Count > 0;
        }
        public static int TasksInTaskSet(string server, int taskset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select count(*) from TaskMap tm where tm.taskset_id = @taskset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@taskset_id", taskset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
        }


        public static DataTable GetAllTaskStatus(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [taskstatus_id], status, cell_color from TaskStatus";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static DataTable GetAllTasks(string server,string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select t.* from vTasksEx t where  t.asset_id = @asset_id and t.latest = 1 ORDER BY default_order ASC";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        public static int CopyTasksFromSet(string server, string asset_id, int taskset_id,int taskstatus_id)
        {
            
            string sql = "exec dbo.CopyTaskSet @asset_id = @asset_id, @taskset_id=@taskset_id, @taskstatus_id=@taskstatus_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@taskset_id", taskset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@taskstatus_id", taskstatus_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<int>();
            
        }

        public static DataTable GetAllTaskSets(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select id [tasktype_id], name from TaskSets";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static void UpdateTask(string server, int task_id,int taskstatus_id,object value,Nullable<DateTime> due_date)
        {
            string sql = "exec dbo.UpdateTaskStatus @task_id=@task_id, @taskstatus_id=@taskstatus_id, @value=@value, @due_date=@due_date";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@task_id", task_id);
            q.AddParameter("@taskstatus_id", taskstatus_id);
            q.AddParameter("@value", value);
            q.AddParameter("@due_date", due_date);
            q.Execute();
        }

    }
}

namespace BadgerLib

        public static DataTable GetCounterpartyTradesAsOf(string server, DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT t.trade_id[trade id]" +
                ", t.trade_date[trade date]" +
                ", t.settle_date[settle date]" +
                ", t.account" +
                ", t.counterparty" +
                ", count(*)[#]" +
                ", sum(t.oface)[investment payment]" +
                ", sum(t.net_proceeds)[proceeds]" +
                ", sum(t.oface * e.exchange_rate) [Exchange Rate x Invs Pmt]" +
            " FROM vTradesEx t" +
                "   JOIN dbo.vAssetsEx e on t.asset_id = e.asset_id" +
                " WHERE t.buy_sell = 'S'" +
                " and t.counterparty_is_unlock = 0" +
                " and t.is_securitization_account_counterparty = 0 " +
                " and t.is_unlock = 1" +
                " and t.is_unlock_buyback_acct = 0 " +
                " and t.trade_date >= @asOf" +
                " GROUP BY t.trade_id, t.trade_date, t.settle_date, t.account, t.counterparty" +
                " ORDER BY t.trade_id desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return tbl;
        }

        public static DataTable GetDailyProductionAsOf(string server, DateTime asOf)
        {
            string sql = "select n.value_date [funding date], count(*) [#], format(sum(n.amount),'N0') [$] " +
                " from dbo.vFundings_New n " +
                " where n.funding_status != 'Cancelled' " +
                "  and n.funding_type = 'Deal' " +
                "  and n.value_date >= @asOf " +
                " group by n.value_date " +
                " order by n.value_date asc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return tbl;
        }

        public static int? GetPayoffTicketID(string server,string asset_id,int? account_id,double oface)
        {
            string sql = "select ticket_id from vTrades t join vAssets a on a.asset_id = t.asset_id where (t.asset_id = @asset_id or a.max_id = try_convert(bigint,@asset_id)) and buy_sell = 'S' and counterparty_id = 0 AND (@account_id is null or t.account_id = @account_id) and t.oface = @oface";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@oface", oface);
            return q.ExecuteSingleNullable<int>("ticket_id");
        }

        public static DataTable GetTradeTape(string server, string which, int? account_id, int? guideline_id_override, int? trade_id, List<string> assets, bool include_paid_off_assets)
        {
            if(null == assets)
                assets = new List<string>();

            string sql = "exec dbo.TapeGen @which=@which,@account_id=@account_id,@guideline_id_override=@guideline_id_override,@trade_id=@trade_id,@assets=@assets,@include_paid_off_assets=@include_paid_off_assets";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@which", which);
            q.AddParameter("@account_id", account_id);
            q.AddParameter("@guideline_id_override", guideline_id_override);
            q.AddParameter("@trade_id", trade_id);
            q.AddParameter("@assets", assets);
            q.AddParameter("@include_paid_off_assets", include_paid_off_assets);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return tbl;
        }

        public static DataTable GetTradeSummary(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select trade_id, trade_date,settle_date, account, counterparty,sum(OFACE) [investment_payment],sum(market_value) [market_value] " +
                "from vTradesEx " +
                "  where is_journal = 0 and is_unlock = 1 and is_unlock_buyback_acct = 0 and buy_sell = 'S' and trade_date >= DATEADD(m, -8, getdate()) and account in ('UPS') group by trade_id,trade_date,settle_date, account, counterparty "  +
                "ORDER BY TRADE_DATE desc";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            DataTable tbl = q.ExecuteTable();
            return tbl;
        }

        public static string GetLocalTradeFolder(string server, int trade_id)
        {
            string base_directory = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, "BASE_TRADES_LOCATION_LOCAL", true);
            string filter = $"*#{trade_id}*";
            var files = System.IO.Directory.GetDirectories(base_directory, filter,SearchOption.AllDirectories);
            if (files.Length == 1)
            {
                string full_path = Path.Combine(base_directory, files[0]);
                return full_path;
            }
            return null;
        }

        public static DataTable GetEligibleCollateral(string server,int account_id, int? guideline_id, bool process_exceptions,bool show_summary, bool show_doc_status, bool show_trade_ticket_copy_paste, bool show_detail, bool show_exception_detail,bool only_eligible,int? @buy_from_acct,bool clear_monday_exceptions)
        {

            Query q = new Query(sql, server);

            q.AddParameter("@guideline_id", guideline_id);
            q.AddParameter("@process_exceptions", process_exceptions);
            q.AddParameter("@show_summary", show_summary);
            q.AddParameter("@show_doc_status", show_doc_status);
            q.AddParameter("@show_trade_ticket_copy_paste", show_trade_ticket_copy_paste);
            q.AddParameter("@show_detail", show_detail);
            q.AddParameter("@show_exception_detail", show_exception_detail);
            q.AddParameter("@only_eligible", only_eligible);

        public static double TotalPositionSize(string server,int account_id)

        public static int AddJournalToTradesTable(string server, DataTable dt, out List<string> assets_removed)
        {
            assets_removed = new List<string>();
            for (int i = dt.Rows.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)
            {
                DataRow dr = dt.Rows[i];
                if (TradeExists(server, dr["ASSET_ID"].ToString()))
                {
                    assets_removed.Add(dr["ASSET_ID"].ToString());
                    dr.Delete();
                }
            }

            List<string> insert_statements = Database.DBUtils.GenerateInsertStatements("Trades", dt, true, true).inserts_raw_dog;
            foreach (string insert in insert_statements)
            {
                Query q = new Query(insert, server);
                q.Execute();
            }
            return insert_statements.Count;
        }

        public static bool TradeExists(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string sql = "select asset_id from vTrades where asset_id = @asset_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.RecordExists();
        }

    }

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Usage.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Usage
    {

        public static class Constants
        {
            public const int STARTUP = 1;
            public const int SHUTDOWN = 2;
        }
        public static void RecordUsage(string server,int usage_id, int? number, int? number_two, string note, string optNote2, string optnote3,int? userID)
        {
            
            DateTime build_time = Assembly.GetCallingAssembly().GetLinkerDateTime(TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById("Eastern Standard Time"));
            string machine = Environment.MachineName;

            string sql = "exec dbo.RecordUsage @usage_id=@usage_id, @number=@number, @number_two=@number_two, @note=@note, @user_id=@user_id, @note2=@note2, @note3=@note3,@build_time=@build_time,@machine=@machine";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@usage_id", usage_id);
            q.AddParameter("@number", number);
            q.AddParameter("@number_two", number_two);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@note2", optNote2);
            q.AddParameter("@note3", optnote3);
            q.AddParameter("@user_id", userID);
            q.AddParameter("@build_time", build_time);
            q.AddParameter("@machine", machine);
            q.ExecuteAsync(null);

        }
    }
}

--- FILE: BadgerLib\Utils.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Utils
    {

        public static string GetAssetNiceName(string server, string asset_id)
        {
            string name_simple = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "name_simple", true);
            string address_full = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "address_full", true);
            string asset_status = BadgerLib.Assets.GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, asset_id, "asset_status", true);

            string title = $"{asset_id} - {name_simple} | {address_full}    [{asset_status}]";
            return title;
        }

        public static DateTime GetCutoffDate(string server)
        {
            return Database.Common.GetGlobal<DateTime>(server, CommonInterfaces.DBGlobals.CUTOFF,false,false);
        }

        public static void SyncInvestorFolders(string server, int account_id, IWriter _writer = null)
        {
            string base_folder = Database.Common.GetGlobal<string>(server, "BASE_INVESTOR_FOLDER", true);
            string acct_name = BadgerLib.Accounts.GetAccountName(server, account_id);
            string final_base_location = Path.Combine(base_folder, acct_name) + "\\Assets\\";
            List<string> assets = BadgerLib.Portfolio.GetAllPositions(server, account_id, true);
            ETA eta = new ETA(assets.Count, _writer);
            foreach(string a in assets)
            {
                string folder = BadgerLib.Assets.LocalFolderLocation(server, a);
                string folder_only = UtilsLib.FileLib.FolderNameOnly(folder);
                string full_target = Path.Combine(final_base_location, folder_only);
                UtilsLib.FileLib.CopyFullDirectory(folder, full_target, null,false, true);
                eta.IncrementAndReport();
            }
            _writer("DONE WITH SYNC!");
            eta.Complete();
        }

    }
}

        {
            string sql = "select * From vValuationsEx v where v.asset_id = @asset_id AND EARLIEST = 1 and primary_avm = 1";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);
        }


        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        
        

        public static int VendorIdFromValuationType(string server, int valuationtype_id)

        public static T GetValuationInfoInternal<T>(string server, int valuationtype_id, string field)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * FROM ValuationTypes vt where vt.id = @valuationtype_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@valuationtype_id", valuationtype_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(field);
        }
        public static void InsertValidation(string server, string asset_id, DateTime asOf, int valuationtype_id, double value, double? value_high, double? value_low, int? confidence, string note, int process_id, int? foreign_process_id, string source_archive, string identifier, string link)
        {
            string sql = "insert into Valuations (asset_id,asOf,valuationtype_id,value,value_high,value_low,confidence,note,process_id,foreign_process_id,source_archive,identifier,link) values (@asset_id,@asOf,@valuationtype_id,@value,@value_high,@value_low,@confidence,@note,@process_id,@foreign_process_id,@source_archive,@identifier,@link)";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@asset_id", asset_id);
            q.AddParameter("@asOf", asOf);
            q.AddParameter("@valuationtype_id", valuationtype_id);
            q.AddParameter("@value", value);
            q.AddParameter("@value_high", value_high);
            q.AddParameter("@value_low", value_low);
            q.AddParameter("@confidence", confidence);
            q.AddParameter("@note", note);
            q.AddParameter("@process_id", process_id);
            q.AddParameter("@foreign_process_id", foreign_process_id);
            q.AddParameter("@source_archive", source_archive);
            q.AddParameter("@identifier", identifier);
            q.AddParameter("@link", link);
            q.Execute();
        }





        public static void ParseAppraisalHack(string server, string asset_id)
        {

        public static double GetStartingValue(List<string> lines)
        {
            double starting_home_value = 0;
            lines.Reverse();
            foreach (string s in lines)
            {
                foreach (string word in s.Split(' '))
                {
                    if (!word.Contains(",000") || word.Contains("1280"))
                        continue;
                    double d;
                    if (Double.TryParse(word, out d))
                    {
                        if (d > 100000)
                        {
                            starting_home_value = d;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (starting_home_value != 0)
                    break;
            }
            return starting_home_value;
        }
        public static void ProcessUniform(string server, string text, string asset_id, string filename)
        {

            string filename_only = Path.GetFileName(filename);
            DateTime? asOf = null;
            if (text.Contains("AS OF"))
            {
                int insp_date = text.IndexOf("AS OF");
                string as_of = text.Substring(insp_date, 50);
                
                asOf = UtilsLib.Clean.FindFirstDateIn(as_of);
                if (null == asOf)
                {
                    if (text.Contains("Which is the date of inspection and the effective date of this appraisal."))
                    {
                        string[] date_sub = text.Split("Which is the date of inspection and the effective date of this appraisal.");
                        string[] last_line = date_sub[0].Split(Environment.NewLine);
                        string last = last_line[last_line.Length - 1];
                        last = last.Replace("asof", "");
                        last = last.Replace("_", "");
                        last = last.Replace(".", "");
                        
                        asOf = UtilsLib.Clean.FindFirstDateIn(last);
                    }
                }
            }

            if (null == asOf)
            {
                if (text.Contains("Effective Date of Appraisal "))
                {
                    int effective = text.IndexOf("Effective Date of Appraisal");
                    string sub_effective = text.Substring(effective - 75, 75);
                    asOf = UtilsLib.Clean.FindFirstDateIn(sub_effective);
                }
            }

            if(null == asOf)
            {
                string substr = text.Substring(0, 800);
                asOf = UtilsLib.Clean.FindFirstDateIn(substr);
            }
            if(null == asOf)
            {
                UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail("uam_sendgrid");
                return;
            }
            
            string[] value = null;
            if (text.Contains("APPRAISED VALUE OF SUBJECT PROPERTY $"))
                value = text.Split("APPRAISED VALUE OF SUBJECT PROPERTY $");
            else
            {
                if(text.Contains("APPRAISED VALUE OF SUBJECT PROPERTY"))
                    value = text.Split("APPRAISED VALUE OF SUBJECT PROPERTY");
            }
            if (null == value || (null != value && value.Length < 1))
                return;
            if (!value[1].Contains("Email Address"))
                return;

            string second_split = value[1].Split("Email Address")[0];
            List<string> lines = new List<string>(second_split.Split(Environment.NewLine));

            string third_split = value[0].Split("Email Address")[0];
            List<string> lines_third = new List<string>(third_split.Split(Environment.NewLine));
            
            double starting_home_value = GetStartingValue(lines);
            if(starting_home_value == 0)
            {
                starting_home_value = GetStartingValue(lines_third);
            }
            if (null == asOf || starting_home_value == 0)
            {
                UtilsLib.Mail m = new UtilsLib.Mail("uam_sendgrid");
                m.SendSMTPMail("dan@unlock.com", null, null, "Failed Parse", filename, null, false, true, null);
                File.AppendAllText(@"C:\trash\appraisal.txt", asset_id);
                return;
            }
            
            {
                bool exists = BadgerLib.Valuations.ValuationsExist(server, asset_id, 19);
                if (!exists)
                {
                    BadgerLib.Valuations.InsertValidation(server, asset_id, asOf.Value, 19, starting_home_value, null, null, null, "Badger Scrape: <no file>", 3, null, filename_only, null, null);
                }
            }
        }
        public static void ProcessSVCLink(string server, string text, string asset_id, string filename)
        {
            string filename_only = Path.GetFileName(filename);
            int insp_date = text.IndexOf("Inspection Date");
            
            string effective_date = text.Substring(insp_date, 40).Split("Inspection Date")[1];
            DateTime asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(effective_date.Split(Environment.NewLine)[0]);
            string file_number = text.Substring(text.IndexOf("File Number"), 20).Split(' ')[2];
            string home_value = text.Substring(text.IndexOf("Effective Date"), 45).Split(' ')[1].Split(Environment.NewLine)[1].Replace("$", "").Replace(",", "");
            int starting_home_value = System.Convert.ToInt32(home_value);
            bool exists = BadgerLib.Valuations.ValuationsExist(server, asset_id, 22);
            if (!exists)
            {
                BadgerLib.Valuations.InsertValidation(server, asset_id, asOf, 22, starting_home_value, null, null, null, "Badger Scrape: " + file_number, 3, null, filename_only, file_number, null);
            }
        }
        public static void ProcessClearVal(string server,string text, string asset_id, string filename)
        {
            string filename_only = Path.GetFileName(filename);
            
            string start_line = " $";
            int index = text.IndexOf(start_line);
            int index_last = text.IndexOf("Loan Number");
            string important = text.Substring(index, index_last - index).Replace(start_line, "");
            string start_val = important.Split(' ')[0].Replace("$", "").Replace(",", "");
            int starting_home_value = System.Convert.ToInt32(start_val);
            string loan_id = important.Split("As-Is Value ")[1].Trim();

            int effective_index_start = text.IndexOf("Effective: ");
            int effective_index_end = text.IndexOf("Client(s): Unlock");
            string effective = text.Substring(effective_index_start, effective_index_end - effective_index_start);
            DateTime asOf = System.Convert.ToDateTime(effective.Split(' ')[1]);
            string property_id = effective.Split(' ')[4];
            
            bool exists = BadgerLib.Valuations.ValuationsExist(server, asset_id, 21);
            if (!exists)
            {
                BadgerLib.Valuations.InsertValidation(server, asset_id, asOf, 21, starting_home_value, null, null, null, "Badger Scrape: " + property_id, 3, null, filename_only, property_id, null);
            }
        }
    }
}


--- FILE: BadgerLib\Vendors.cs ---
namespace BadgerLib
{
    public class Vendors
    {



        public static async Task<DataTable> GetAllVendors(string server,int vendortype_id)
        {
            string sql = "select id [vendor_id],vendortype_id,name from Vendors where vendortype_id = @vendortype_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@vendortype_id", vendortype_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return await q.ExecuteTableTask();
        }

        public static DataTable GetVendorsByUsage(string server, int vendorusage_id)
        {
            string sql = "select vendor_id,name [vendor_name] from vVendorsEx where vendorusage_id = @vendorusage_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@vendorusage_id", vendorusage_id);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }

        public static Dictionary<int,string> GetVendorSupportNames(string server)
        {
            string sql = "select vendor_id,full_short from vVendorsEx where support_email is not null";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.UseCache = true;
            return q.ExecuteDictRows<int, string>("vendor_id", "full_short");
        }

        public static string SupportEmail(string server,int vendor_id)
        {
            return GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, vendor_id, "support_email", true);
        }

        public static string EmailCC(string server, int vendor_id)
        {
            return GetSingleAttribute<string>(server, vendor_id, "email_cc", true);
        }
        public static T GetSingleAttribute<T>(string server, int vendor_id, string db_field, bool use_cache)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vVendors a where a.vendor_id = @vendor_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@vendor_id", vendor_id);
            q.UseCache = use_cache;
            T t = q.ExecuteSingle<T>(db_field);

            return t;
        }
    }
}

namespace BadgerLib
{
    public static class Watchlist
    {

        public static DataTable GetWatchlist(string server)
        {
            string sql = "SELECT * from vWatchlist";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
        public static T GetAttributeInternal<T>(string server, int watchlist_id, string attribute)
        {
            string sql = "select * from vWatchlist where watchlist_id = @watchlist_id";
            Query q = new Query(sql, server);
            q.AddParameter("@watchlist_id", watchlist_id);
            return q.ExecuteSingle<T>(attribute);
        }

        public static DataTable GetWatchlistTable(string server, int months_back, double threshold_pct, double coll_thresh,List<int> accts)
        {
            Query q = new Query("Watchlist.sql", server);
            q.AddParameter("@months_back", months_back);
            q.AddParameter("@threshold_pct", threshold_pct);
            q.AddParameter("@coll_thresh", coll_thresh);
            q.AddParameter("@accts", accts);

            
            return q.ExecuteTable();
        }
    }
}
